Current Affairs Commentary

Pay Attention to Post-Suppression Work When Suppressing the Bandits in Ludong

— Shi

Since the Tanggu Accord was established, the crisis has gradually eased. However, there are still many thorns ahead. Post-disaster work is not easy. The dispersal and loss of the passionate youths from the four provinces due to patriotism are minor matters. Since 4.3 million square miles of land has fallen into foreign hands, customs duties have decreased by 20 million yuan per year. The people who were invisibly imported into the Shandong and Hebei provinces from the northeast have also been cut off. Furthermore, in counties like Ludong, agriculture is not very fertile and industry is not fully developed. The reason they are more prosperous than the counties in northern Hebei is the invisible imports from the three northeastern provinces. Recently, the situation has changed drastically. Not only has this kind of invisible import disappeared, but also large numbers of refugees from outside the pass have poured in. In addition, the enemy and puppet bandits have been ravaged or alienated and provoked, creating trouble for no reason. Therefore, entanglements are emerging and handling them is thorny.

The various counties of Ludong, while Sino-Japanese disputes are unresolved, are regions with significant risks in general political relations. Li Jichun's troops have just been reorganized and the dispute has come to an end. The Lao Haozi gang has risen again, which seems to be a minor ailment and unrelated to the overall situation. However, upon careful examination, its reality is complex and contains future crises. If there are no thorough solutions, it is feared that future troubles will be left behind. Lao Haozi and others were originally part of the Northeast Volunteer Army, raising their arms against Japan. Later, because the Volunteer Army retreated westward or went into hiding on the spot, the overall strategy has changed. Therefore, some people inevitably defected and were taken advantage of by the enemy, and even provided with weapons and ammunition, and assisted with funds. This situation is very dangerous. Moreover, all parts of Jidong have repeatedly suffered from war disasters and the people are still in dire straits. The Japanese army within Hebei is still staying and has not withdrawn. Most social mentalities are still uneasy. As for Liu Guitang, Tang Yulin, and other troops, they are still stationed inside Dushikou and the Chicheng area. Without concrete resettlement methods, or if the handling is accidentally inappropriate, it will easily provoke latent crises, and the localities will again be ravaged.

Furthermore, the provinces and regions in the Yellow River Basin were civilized earlier in our country, but they are still stuck in an agricultural economy. The hub of commercial development is in trade with Mongolia and doing business with the three northeastern provinces. This is the case for Shanxi commerce, and it is also the case for Tianjin merchants. However, since Outer Mongolia seceded and the northeast was lost, the road to business has been blocked. The world economic panic has struck, and militarism has been forced into it. Commercial capital, which only engages in transshipment, has had to painfully sacrifice it. Agricultural management in our country has already exhausted its greatest ability in manual labor to engage in cultivation. However, over the past thousands of years, the land has been completely depleted of its power. If artificial fertilization is not added in the future, it will be difficult to hope for an increase in production. We try to observe the provinces of Hebei, Shandong, Shanxi, and Henan in detail. More than 90% of the cultivated land currently cultivated has been withered. The phosphorus and other vitality contained in the land are gradually lacking. The depletion can be known without waiting for chemical analysis. Looking again at the residents of the Yellow River Basin, most of them show signs of hunger. Only one or two out of a hundred can truly have enough food and a little surplus strength. Since farming cannot make up for the current urgent needs and the land is becoming increasingly depleted, if no method is devised to provide relief, and hoping that they will be able to regenerate with their own strength, I am afraid there will be no day for it.

Therefore, the plan for today cannot only seek temporary peace in upper-level politics, but should, in a negative aspect, first resolve all political contradictions, so that the existing troops can become national troops and not hinder the upward development of productive undertakings. If it can turn soldiers into workers and relocate them to the border, it will be transformed from pure consumption to production. This can be a benefit for ten years in political terms, and economic development can also be slightly developed. Taking a further step to plan large-scale intensive agricultural management, the provinces of Hebei and Shandong may be able to get some help. In a positive aspect, we must pay attention to the development of the cotton and wool industries. Our country has abundant raw materials and a wide consumer market. We only need to be able to use scientific methods and apply artificial fertilizers to cultivate the soil, and it will not be difficult to gradually prosper the agriculture of the northern provinces. The people will be able to settle down in their business, and the economy will also be able to develop upwards. Once the root of the disturbance is settled, it will be able to generate resistance to the outside world.

Japan's Drug Crisis, Northeast China Issue: Situation Changes at League of Nations Conference; British Representative Accommodates the Status Quo and Proposes Amendment, Passed by the Assembly with Enthusiastic Support from Japanese Representative

(Geneva) The Advisory Committee continued to discuss the opium issue this afternoon, and the situation has changed. Sir John ডেvenham, the British representative to the Geneva International Opium Conference, proposed an amendment, which was enthusiastically supported by the Japanese representative Yokoyama and passed unanimously by the Assembly. Sir John ডেvenham proposed adding the following to the report: "The former Manchurian administrators had used opium production and taxation schemes to generate huge revenues. The new administrators seem to want to establish a monopoly to increase tax revenues. Recent information received about opium causes great anxiety, because the new situation will not only expand drug abuse locally, but will also endanger other countries. The committee has noted the establishment of secret factories in the Far East and other places, where large quantities of opium are available for use, and Manchuria will also face the same danger. Because the League of Nations Council has not recognized the new Manchurian administrators, it has not received reports and other information from the parts stipulated in the convention. Therefore, the committee feels that it should take the most appropriate method for the current situation to meet the needs of the Council, so as to seek detailed information on the production, sale, and use of drugs in Manchuria, and handle everything in the same way as receiving reports from other countries. The current administrators of Manchuria should know that their opium policy has a great impact on other countries and should know that it is now necessary to cooperate in implementing all the restrictions that other countries have agreed to abide by. This is crucial and cannot be ignored." The Belgian representative accepted ডেvenham's amendment and proposed adding the following paragraph: "At present, we would like to ask opium exporting countries to pay attention to all applications for opium and narcotics to these places, and it is necessary to implement extremely strict management." The Italian representative proposed voting on the text proposed by the Belgian representative, but it was rejected by the assembly with nine votes against six. Therefore, ডেvenham's amendment was passed unanimously. (Reuters, 3rd)

(Geneva) Since the opening of the League of Nations Opium Advisory Committee, people in the League of Nations have been discussing whether the widespread planting of poppies in Manchuria will lead to the possibility of the powerful countries de facto recognizing the puppet organization. Because Japan has not signed the international convention on the control of drugs, and "Manchukuo" is not bound by any international agreements, all committee members believe that it is very difficult to collect opium statistics from Manchuria. Therefore, the committee has suggested that the League of Nations Council find a way to obtain a complete report on the production and sale of opium in Manchuria. Although the committee stated that its only purpose is to reduce the opium trade and that it has never put the international political situation in its mind, the League of Nations representatives immediately saw that this suggestion had the possibility of tending towards de facto recognition, because there is no other way to obtain the necessary statistics. Moreover, in the current situation, Manchuria has created an opium monopoly and is also planting opium extensively, which will inevitably cause endless harm. Therefore, the committee stated in its suggestion that this uncontrolled and unreported opium harvest will easily become a threat to the world. (National News Agency, 3rd)

The So-Called Araki-Style Outline for a Peace Conference Aims to Recognize Japan's Policy of Aggression Against China; The Military Proposes an Agenda Divided into Seven Major Items

Hua-Lian News Agency Tokyo Correspondence According to the Tokyo Nichi Nichi Shimbun, Minister of War Araki, in order to cope with the crisis of 1936, has decided to propose to the government to promote the East Asian Peace Conference. Minister of War Araki's proposal is as follows: (1) The time should be before the Second London Conference in 1935. (2) The meeting place is set in Tokyo. (3) Japan is the initiator and sends invitations to East Asian countries. (4) The participating countries are Japan, the United States, Russia, China, the United Kingdom, India, France, the Netherlands, Manchukuo, and others. (5) The purpose of the meeting is to determine East Asian peace, liquidate all past disputes, and determine the outline of East Asian peace work. (6) Scope of discussion: (1) "Recognition of Manchukuo" The purpose of Japan's withdrawal from the League of Nations is to enable all countries to recognize the independence of Manchukuo. Recognition of Manchukuo is a basic condition for peace in the Far East. This conference should allow Manchukuo to participate. The issue of Manchukuo's recognition must be resolved at this conference, so Manchukuo's participation is an absolute condition. (2) "Naval Treaty Issue" The purpose of this conference is to liquidate various treaties in East Asia. The preparatory conditions for the Washington and London conferences must be decided at this conference. (3) "Kellogg-Briand Pact and Nine-Power Treaty" Since the Manchurian Incident, these two treaties have been the object of dispute between the two sides. This conference must revise new treaties in accordance with the new situation in East Asia. (4) "Japanese-Russian Non-Aggression Treaty" This conference is convened to resolve future international relations. Therefore, the Japanese-Russian non-aggression treaty must first resolve all the root causes of disputes between the two countries, such as the Sino-Eastern Railway and the Japanese-Russian fishery issue, which should also be resolved in connection with this issue. (5) "China Issue" The East Asian Peace Conference should examine the China issue, based on the Shanghai and North China cease-fire agreements, resolve all disputes, and simultaneously resolve issues such as commercial treaties, tariff issues, extraterritorial rights, and all outstanding issues. It should take Sino-Japanese friendship as the basis and determine East Asian peace work. (6) "India Issue" The economic problems between Japan and India must be fundamentally resolved. (7) "League of Nations Issue" If the issue of recognizing Manchukuo is resolved, then Japan's issue with the League of Nations will also be resolved naturally. Minister of War Araki is scheduled to return to Tokyo at the end of the month and consult with Minister of the Navy Osumi, and then make a suggestion to the government.

Unfortunately, some people are now campaigning against it. Resolutions made under the Locarno Treaty must be made by the League of Nations Council, and the votes of the League of Nations Council must be unanimous. Therefore, since Britain is a permanent director of the Council, a vote cannot be passed without British consent. But there is one exception: if Britain encounters a breach of the undertaking not to go to war or an invasion of the demilitarized zone of the Rhineland, it must provide assistance to the injured party. But even if Britain encounters such a situation, it is still the sole judge of whether this obligation is applicable. The Locarno Treaty does not contain clauses allowing contracting states to withdraw from the alliance. If Britain withdraws, Britain will be more likely to be drawn into European wars than when the Locarno Treaty exists. We must know that the policy of isolation is a foolish policy. Germany's withdrawal from the disarmament conference has made the situation more difficult, but disarmament work must still proceed. Britain is determined to avoid an arms race. (Reuters, 3rd)

U.S. Willing to Cooperate with Britain and France to Maintain Financial Stability; Reiterates No Intention to Cause a Currency War; Foreign Gold Purchase Plan Underway; Quantity and Price Kept Secret

(Washington) U.S. government officials today denied any intention to undermine world financial stability, saying they will use cooperative methods to maintain it. Although the New York Federal Reserve Bank has full discretion to purchase any amount of gold at any price abroad, it will still cooperate with the Bank of England and the Bank of France to achieve financial stability. This cooperation can be expanded to include commercial banks in both countries. The foreign gold purchase plan is already underway. As for the exact amount and price, the Financial Reconstruction Corporation has changed its initial plan to keep it secret and not disclose it. However, the U.S. government has made it clear that it has no intention of causing a currency war, and some of the president's advisors have always advocated sound money, so the market's fears have been somewhat relieved. Now, there is an expectation that the price of the gold dollar will gradually depreciate abroad to reach the desired level. (National News Agency, 3rd)

(Washington) The United States is keeping the purchase of gold abroad strictly secret for two reasons: first, to avoid other countries being drawn into a currency war; and second, to keep speculators from knowing the truth. The U.S. decision not to announce the daily gold purchase price naturally has other reasons. The U.S. authorities do not want to explicitly show outsiders what they are doing. Furthermore, observing various phenomena, in addition to raising the price of gold, the U.S. authorities at least want to stabilize the exchange rate between the U.S. dollar, the British pound, and the French franc, but do not want to make this exchange rate fixed. Anglo-American Negotiations Fail to Agree on Permanent War Debt Arrangement; Future Talks in Washington Can Only Seek Understanding on Payments Due

(Washington) Today, British sources here stated that the British representative, Sir Frederick Leith-Ross, was very disappointed that the Anglo-American war debt conference had broken down on the issue of negotiating a permanent agreement and is now preparing to return home, leaving the negotiations for the December payment to others. The proposals that led to the failure of the conference are currently being kept secret. Today, only Undersecretary of the Treasury Acheson claimed that efforts to discuss a permanent solution have been abandoned, and future talks will focus on understanding regarding the debt due in December. However, legal experts say that the U.S. President's authority to accept silver will expire before mid-November. If Britain does not pay early, this method will be difficult to consider. Some officials believe that Britain will use some method to pay a certain amount to show good faith, and the United States is expected to accept whatever method the British offer. Although no detailed information was released on the previous negotiations, it is said that even if Britain had a concrete proposal, it would not be announced at this time, because before the conference began, it was widely rumored that the British representative would ask for a 90% reduction in the total debt, and the U.S. government also made it clear that such debt reduction would be rejected by Congress. The actual talks between the U.S. Treasury Secretary and the British representative have been few and short, often lasting only half an hour. Three days ago, the U.S. President personally met with the British representative. The details of the talks at that time were not released. It is now believed that the meeting was very important and was probably the basis for judging the fate of the negotiations. However, it is speculated that although the two sides are still far apart on the amount of debt relief, there may have been important results in the monetary field, because monetary issues must have been discussed at that time, and the news confirmed today that the New York Reserve Bank will cooperate with the Bank of England to maintain financial stability is enough to show that the talks that day were not without results. (National News Agency, 3rd)

(Washington) Today, since Treasury Secretary Acheson claimed that the Anglo-American war debt negotiations have temporarily abandoned the discussion of a permanent agreement and will only continue to discuss the December payment method, general attention has focused on the war debt issue, and it is said that the Treasury Department is now considering issuing silver certificates using the one thousand U.S. dollars in silver paid by the United Kingdom in June as a reserve. Overview of Japanese Railway Management in Manchukuo; Railway General Bureau Fully Manages Manchurian Railway; Manchukuo Currently Has Approximately 6,000 Kilometers of Railways; Plan to Build Approximately 4,000 Kilometers More Within Ten Years

According to Japanese newspaper reports, since March 1 of this year, after the railways in Manchukuo were entrusted to the South Manchuria Railway (SMR) Company by the puppet authorities, the SMR authorities began to pour in their years of experience to carry out the improvement, connection, and coordination of various railway operations, in order to smoothly implement transportation control. Since the implementation of entrusted management, the SMR Company has established the Railway General Bureau in Shenyang to manage all administrative matters and is currently proceeding step by step with the improvement of existing railways and the construction of new lines, in order to complete the Manchukuo railway network. The railways entrusted to the SMR Company by puppet Manchukuo include the Jichang, Jidun, Jihui, Sitao, Taoang, Taosuo, Qike, Huhai (including a part of the Songhua River waterway business), Shenhai, and Fengshan (including the Datong line and affiliated ports) completed railways. The total amount of loans is 130 million yuan. Other lines, such as the one between Dunhua and Tumenjiang, have also been completed. The line between Changchun and Tumenjiang has also been opened, which is the so-called Jingtu Line. The SMR also designated Rajin in North Korea as a port for goods entering and exiting North Manchuria, adopting the principle of using the three ports of Jinjin, Qingjin, and Unggi in conjunction, and connecting it with the Jingguo Line, the entrusted management line.

Japanese Railway Policy Toward Manchukuo

Japan's policies regarding transportation issues in Manchuria are two-fold: (1) Major railways take the principle of national operation, with economic development as the main focus. For the purpose of national defense and maintaining security, the total length of future railway lines is targeted at 25,000 kilometers, with the expectation of newly building 4,000 kilometers in the next ten years and merging the existing railways into 10,000 kilometers. (According to the existing railway lines, the total length of the Railway General Bureau Line is more than 3,100 kilometers, the South Manchuria Railway Company Line is more than 1,100 kilometers, and the Chinese Eastern Railway is more than 1,700 kilometers, totaling approximately 6,000 kilometers.) (2) For economic connection between production areas and seaports, in addition to domestic ports, the ports of neighboring countries are also utilized. (Note: "Domestic" here refers to puppet Manchukuo, and "neighboring countries" refers to Japan.) The naval policy prioritizes coastal routes and then ocean routes. Modification work is being carried out in Yingkou and Andong ports, and the Rongludao port construction plan is being prepared to improve the South Manchuria Railway-centric principle.

Current Railway Length in the Puppet State of Manchukuo

According to Mr. Kan'ichi Usami, Director-General of the Railway Bureau, the current railway density in Manchuria, calculated based on Manchuria's area of 1.2 million square kilometers and the total length of existing railways at 6,000 kilometers, is approximately 0.5 kilometers per 100 square kilometers. In Japan, this figure is 5.4 kilometers per 100 square kilometers. Even considering Japan and Korea together, the figure is 1.5 kilometers, which is three times greater than Manchuria's density. Therefore, there is a real need for constructing new lines in Manchuria. Currently, besides the Dunhua-Tumen line and the Laibin line, lines such as the one entering Jehol from Beining and the Haike line connecting Hailar and Qiqihar have already begun provisional operation. Other lines under construction total approximately 750 kilometers. The Jehol line will soon reach Chengde and Chifeng, and the Haike line is planned to extend northward to the Dalikhe River, opposite Blagoveshchensk. If these railway plans proceed smoothly, it is estimated that the railway network in Manchuria can be doubled within ten years.

Water Transport and Automobile Transportation

In addition to railways, the Railway Bureau also manages water transport and automobile businesses. Specifically, water transport on the Songhua River, Yalu River, Liao River, and other rivers is managed by the Railway Bureau. Manchurian ships have, starting this year, entered the main stream of the Heilongjiang River from the Songhua River, reaching Daheihe. Further development in the future is predictable. Furthermore, the automobile business under the new management format has become inseparable from the railway business. Separating them would only result in losses for both sides, as has been seen in Europe, America, and Japan. The South Manchuria Railway authorities, mindful of this, have taken over the full management of all automobile businesses except those with year-round connections to the railway. The automobile route between Beining and Chaoyang, which began operation on March 20th of this year, is the first example of this. Currently, it directly reaches Chengde. The passenger and freight transport service on the Chifeng line will also start soon. This is just one example. In the future, as the so-called 50,000-kilometer national highway plan of the puppet state of Manchukuo steadily progresses, the transportation system will become more complete than it is today, with automobile traffic in various places closely connected to the railway.

Establishing Railway Villages Along Railway Lines

The Railway Bureau employs approximately 40,000 people, mostly Manchurians. To foster harmony and closeness between employees and residents along the railway lines, the authorities are establishing railway villages along the lines. Within these villages, they provide improved grain seeds, raise livestock such as pigs and sheep to improve their breeds, and use various means to maintain cooperation between the people and the railway. They aim to ensure that the people benefit from the Railway Bureau's support, thus inspiring them to cherish the railway. (World News Agency)

Insider Story of the Daishing Corporation of the Puppet State: Merging Former Official Subsidiary Businesses into an Organization for Profiteering from the People

Harbin dispatch: The Daishing Corporation of the puppet state has been reported on by newspapers inside the pass in the past four or five months. Some have described its significance as being equal to the East India Company operated by the British in India, while others have referred to it as a joint mining enterprise between Japan and the puppet state. In reality, both are inaccurate. The Daishing Corporation originates from the merging of various subsidiary businesses of former official financial institutions in the three northeastern provinces, including the Official Bank of the Three Eastern Provinces, Yongheng Official Bank, Heilongjiang Official Bank, Border Industry Bank, and the Bank of the Three Eastern Provinces. Before the fall of the Northeast, these official financial institutions also operated subsidiary businesses such as grain shops, oil mills, and flour mills to connect with the social economy and support the market. After the fall of the Northeast, when the puppet Central Bank was established, all the official banks were incorporated into it. The former subsidiary businesses, which were used to support the development of the banking business, were reorganized into an industry bureau for operation. This bureau annually purchased grain and planned enterprises, with all activities aimed at generating profits for the bank falling within its scope. The oil mills, flour mills, and other subsidiary institutions, due to their existing nature and planned operations, were incorporated into the Daishing Corporation. Therefore, the Daishing Corporation is a unique part of the bank, unlike the previous situation where the banks themselves operated subsidiary businesses. The corporation's organization resembles a joint investment partnership between Japan and the puppet state, with existing assets valued at 25 million, supplemented by a Japanese investment of 25 million, totaling 50 million silver dollars. However, although the existing assets have been valued, the Japanese investment has not actually contributed a single penny. The corporation has a board of directors, with the chairman being Wang Huihai, the former assistant manager of the Jilin Yongheng Official Bank. Below him are two Japanese and puppet directors, and one resident Japanese director. Managers of local flour mills, oil mills, and pawnshops are all managed by one director. The corporation was officially established in early September of this year. The organization of the corporation may seem insignificant on the surface, but in reality, it is a mechanism for concentrating power, absorbing small capital, and exploiting the rural economy. In the future, within a year, the financial lifeline of farmers in the Northeast will be controlled by this corporation. Farmers, facing economic decline, will inevitably rely on the corporation for assistance and material supplies. Therefore, the corporation's substantial authority is no less than that of the East India Company.

(November 1st)

Military Tension in the Sichuan-Hubei Border Region Due to Bandit Suppression; Xu's Bandits Rampant, Sichuan Situation Worsens; Kuang and He Gangs Also Plot to Flee into Sichuan Territory

Hankou dispatch: Since Xu Xiangqian's bandit gang entered Sichuan, occupying the three counties of Tongnanba, and then capturing Peng'an, Qu County, Yingshan, Suiding, and Xuanhan, the situation in Sichuan has been deteriorating daily. The He Long and Kuang Jixun gangs, which have been harassing the border regions of Hunan, Hubei, Henan, and Anhui, have also become active. Recently, they have even attempted to enter Sichuan in separate routes and join forces with Xu's bandits. The bandit suppression situation has undergone a significant change. Initially, after Xu's bandits occupied the three counties, under the planning of Liu Bocheng, the former chief of staff of Zhu De, they took advantage of the fact that Liu Xiang had not yet taken office and the Sichuan provincial troops were disorganized. They led their forces in a sudden attack, capturing Yang Sen's defense areas of Peng'an, Qu County, and Yingshan. Subsequently, they sent troops north, capturing Xuanhan and Suiding, inflicting a major blow on Liu Cunhou. The bandits' plan was to defeat Tian Songyao, Deng Xihou, Yang Sen, and Liu Cunhou individually, and then attack Liu Xiang with all their strength. Unfortunately, the weaknesses of the Sichuan army were exploited by the bandits. These weaknesses include: (1) After Liu Xiang took office as commander-in-chief of bandit suppression in Sichuan, he was unable to effectively command the various units of Deng, Tian, Liu, and Yang. (2) The generals were suspicious of each other, their strength was weak, and the soldiers were unpaid and unwilling to fight to the death. (3) Liu Xiang and others routinely imposed heavy taxes, with taxes already collected up to the 67th year of the Republic of China, causing widespread resentment among the people, making them easily incited. Thus, the bandits' advance was like crushing dry weeds. After the bandits captured Sui and Xuan, they expanded their strength, organizing themselves into four armies, with He Wei and others serving as army commanders, plotting to invade eastern Sichuan and threaten Yuwan. Liu Xiang, realizing the urgency of the situation, immediately returned to Chongqing to deploy defenses and ordered Tang Shizun's troops to guard along the Yangtze River, gradually stabilizing public sentiment. Liu then issued a martial law order for eastern Sichuan on the same day and set off for Chengdu on the second day. On the third day, he convened the generals to give instructions and decided to depart for Suining on the fourth day, issuing general suppression orders to all routes. However, the troops of each army were still not in good order. Liu Cunhou is currently consolidating his troops in Liangshan, making it difficult for him to take on one side again. Tian Songyao is stationed in Langzhong and Cangxi, barely able to defend himself. Deng Xihou has been designated to send troops to Zhaohua and Guangyuan but is still on his way to Shunqing. Although Yang Sen has telegraphed that he has recovered Yingshan, this has yet to be confirmed. Therefore, the so-called large-scale encirclement by six routes still requires factual proof to be credible. He Long's remaining bandits have been fleeing in the border region of Hunan and Hubei for the past few months. They were pursued by Governor Xu Yuanquan and unable to establish a foothold. Seeing Xu's bandits gaining momentum in Sichuan, they planned to join forces. A month ago, they entered Sichuan in three routes but were blocked by the Sichuan army and fled back to Hubei. They are now entrenched in the Xiaomo Creek, Pangzu River, and Huolongping area on the border between Lichuan in Hubei and Qianjiang in Sichuan, still plotting to enter Sichuan at an opportune moment. According to Xu Yuanquan's telegram of the third day, the bandits' internal structure has disintegrated. Duan Dechang, Duan Yulin, and Wang Bingnan, three bandit leaders, were all killed on suspicion of being members of the reorganization faction. Xia Xi seized the position of chairman of the Hunan-Hubei-Western Soviet government. He Long, Guan Wenying, Song Panming, Lu Dongsheng, Ye Guangji, and Chen Peiyin are members of the committee. Ye and Chen have since been killed, and Lu has been injured by bombing. The bandits' main force has been defeated by our army and is expected to be eliminated in the short term. However, the bandits are elusive, and preventing them from entering Sichuan is not easy. Furthermore, the remaining forces of Kuang Jixun on the border of Henan, Hubei, and Anhui are being suppressed by Liu Zhenhua, who is leading the troops of Sun Lianzhong, Liang Guanying, Shangguan Yunxiang, Hao Mengling, Wan Yaohuang, Peng Zhenshan, Song Tiancai, and Dai Minquan in separate routes. The bandit areas have mostly been recovered, and the remaining bandits, in a state of distress, are also planning to flee into Sichuan. One morning, at Xin'an Store between Minggang and Queshan on the southern section of the Pinghan Railway, a large group of six to seven thousand bandits crossed the railway and fled west. It is reported that they are the 25th and 28th armies of the gang, who first gathered in Zhengyang, crossed the railway, intending to pass through Biyang, Tang County, Nanyang, Zhechuan, and follow the upper reaches of the Han River, passing through Shaanxi and entering Sichuan's Chengkou and then Wanyuan. It is also reported that the local bandits of Biyang and Tongbai, Xiao Liushao and Gu Da 　　(Continued on page 9)

Page 9

Sheng, after being severely suppressed by Xiao Zhichu's troops, also have a tendency to join forces with the bandits and flee into Sichuan. Considering the situation from all sides, Sichuan has become a haven for disaster bandits. If the generals in Sichuan do not join forces to suppress them, allowing them to grow stronger, the disaster of a prairie fire will be even more difficult to extinguish. (November 3rd)

Strength of Various Armies in Sichuan Province: Total Reduction of 40,000 Troops; Liu Wenhui's Army Remaining at Approximately 30,000

Chongqing dispatch: The Sichuan army, in its heyday, was claimed to be 500,000 strong. In reality, after thorough calculation of all units, the number was more than that, totaling over 600,000. Since the two Sichuan civil wars, the various armies have suffered losses of no less than 100,000. However, the number of reinforcements has been over 150,000 to 160,000. Liu Xiang, the commissioner of good governance of Sichuan, has recently advocated for troop reduction, so the strength of the various armies has undergone some changes. A brief account is as follows:

Deng Xihou

Deng Xihou's 28th Army originally had approximately 40-odd regiments. Later, due to changes in the situation in Sichuan, it gradually expanded to over 50 regiments. During the recent military resurgence in Sichuan, Deng's forces participated fully, absorbing the remaining units of the 24th Army, approximately 20-odd regiments, thus expanding to between 78 and 80 regiments. However, the organization of the divisions, brigades, regiments, and companies was often understaffed. On average, each regiment had approximately 6,000 to 7,000 men, totaling 50,000. Weapons and equipment were quite scarce. With a narrow defense area, the monthly military expenditure was insufficient, at less than 300,000. After Deng expressed his support for Liu Xiang, Liu ordered the army to reduce its size to 40 regiments and promised to provide 150,000 in monthly financial assistance, to be allocated by the commissioner's office. Deng then convened a meeting of all army generals to discuss the issue of troop reduction. After several discussions, it was decided to reduce the entire army to 50 regiments, with the troops of the former 3rd Division commander Chen Shunong being reorganized into 12 regiments, the 2nd Division Huang Yimin's troops into 9 regiments, the 7th Division Ma Dezai's troops into 9 regiments, the Training Division Chen Jingshan's troops into 6 regiments, the Independent Division Yang Xiuchun's troops into 6 regiments, and the 5 Mixed Brigades Xie Decan's troops being reduced to 4 regiments. Deng Xihou's directly controlled independent commanders Huang Ao and Niu Fanjiu's troops were combined into 4 regiments. Each regiment was limited to three battalions, each battalion to three companies, and each company to three platoons, with 30 men per platoon, totaling approximately 40,000 men. With the 150,000 in funding from Liu Xiang, they are still able to maintain the current situation.

Tian Songyao

Tian Songyao's 29th Army, in its heyday, totaled 60 regiments and four companies. During the Sichuan civil war last year, the various units of the army actively expanded, appointing a large number of officers and recruiting from all directions, attempting to follow in the footsteps of the 24th Army and build up a force of 100 regiments. As the army possessed the Chengdu Arsenal for many years, and each division also had small-scale repair shops, they did not feel a shortage of weapons and ammunition, making expansion easier. However, the army suffered heavy losses in the Chengdu battle and now has over 30 regiments remaining, including the 1st Division Dong Changan's troops with 4 regiments, the 2nd Division Zeng Nanfu's troops with 9 regiments, the 3rd Division Luo Naiqiong's troops with 4 regiments, the 4th Division Wang Mingzhang's troops with 2 regiments, the 5th Division Huang Futang's troops with 4 regiments, the Independent Division Liu Hanxiong's troops with 3 regiments, the 1st Route Commander Li Wei's troops with 2 regiments, the 3rd Route Commander He Zhanru's troops with 2 regiments, the 4th Route Commander Yang Jie's troops with 2 regiments, the 5th Route Commander Wang Zhiyuan's troops with 2 regiments, the Special Service Commander Tian Zefu's troops with 2 regiments, the Independent Commander Ye Jishi's troops with 1-odd regiment, and the Supervisor Commander Han Guozhu with 1-odd regiment. The above units are calculated according to their current numbers, but in reality, the units of the army have many vacancies, with some regiments reduced to one or two battalions, some battalions reduced to one or two companies, and some companies reduced to 50 to 60 soldiers. Among them, Zeng Nanfu's troops are relatively well-manned, while Wang Mingzhang's troops suffered the greatest losses. In each county of the Chengdu area, the army collected grain a total of twelve times, once a month, under the name of "Sun and Moon Donation." Recently, the army's monthly military expenditure has been insufficient by about two-thirds. Liu Xiang has promised to allocate 150,000 in monthly funding to the army but has limited the various units of the army to a total of 36 regiments, abolishing the brigade commander level, with the regiment as the combat unit. Above the regiment is the route, and above the route is the division. Each route commands two regiments, each division commands three regiments, and each regiment is prescribed 800 men, with the entire army totaling approximately 30,000 men.

Yang Sen

Yang Sen's 20th Army receives 100,000 in monthly funding from Liu Xiang. The army is currently planning to reorganize its entire force into three divisions, with Yu Mengji as the commander of the 1st Division, Yang Hanyu as the commander of the 1st Division, and Long Huanzhang as the commander of the 3rd Division. Each division commands three brigades, each brigade commands three regiments, each regiment commands three battalions, each battalion commands three companies, and each regiment is authorized 8,000 men, totaling 27 regiments, with approximately 21,000 men, and eliminating approximately 5,000 soldiers.

Liu Cunhou

Liu Cunhou's 23rd Army originally had only two divisions, totaling 20 regiments, with approximately 20,000 men. They were defeated by the Red bandits this time, leaving only 8,000-odd men. They are currently being consolidated.

Li Qixiang

Li Qixiang's New 6th Division and Sichuan Border Defense Commander, after relying on Liu Xiang, had a force of 10,000 men. During the recent military resurgence in Sichuan, Li absorbed a total of nine regiments from the 24th Army, thus expanding the troops to nearly 20,000. Liu Xiang was quite jealous of this and specifically limited the unit to 15,000, otherwise, he would stop providing food and salary. Li had no choice but to comply and is now reorganizing the entire unit into five brigades, with Li Dedong, Chen Shaotang, Wu Shengqing, Li Zongfang, and Ma Ciyu serving as brigade commanders, with each brigade averaging approximately 3,000 men.

Luo Zezhou

Luo Zezhou's 23rd Division originally had over 7,000 troops and has now also increased to 14,000 men. Liu Xiang ordered the dismissal of 4,000 men, leaving only 10,000 men. Luo has complied with the order.

Liu Xiang

In summary, the total number of troops reduced from the above units is approximately 40,000. All 40,000 of the dismissed soldiers were not actually discharged, but were completely recruited by Liu Xiang's 21st Army. Thus, the 21st Army has recently increased sharply from 110,000 to over 160,000.

Liu Wenhui

Liu Wenhui of the 24th Army, in his heyday, commanded 100,000 troops, occupying over 70 counties in central Sichuan. He was strong in both military power and wealth and could have achieved great things. However, due to improper measures in recent years, he lost the sympathy of the various armies, leading to last year's war. As a result, he lost over 30 counties of territory and suffered a loss of 20,000 troops. Despite the defeat, he still had over 80,000 rifles, over 900 machine guns, over 600 mortars, and over 20 boxes of hand grenades, and a territory of over 30 counties. This spring, the Sichuan war broke out again. The entire army was defeated, with those who surrendered surrendering and those who rebelled rebelling. Liu only led the remaining thousand-odd men and fled to Hanyuan in a panic. He telegraphed Liu Xiang for peace, which ended the dispute. The Yuya area remains as a defense area. Currently, there are approximately 30,000 troops in total. Liu issues orders in the name of the Sichuan-Xikang Border Defense Commander and has appointed Xiang Yuren as the deputy commander-in-chief, commanding the entire army. He has appointed Wang Yuanhu as the commander of the 1st Division, Tian Boshi as the commander of the 2nd Division, Xu Tingxiu as the commander of the 3rd Division, Deng Pancun as the commander of the 4th Division, Li Yushu as the commander of the 5th Division, Liu Yuantang as the commander of the 6th Division, and Liu Yuanzhang as the commander of the 7th Division. He has also appointed Tang Ying as the Xikang Reclamation Commander. The entire army has seven divisions and two commander positions, and is actively expanding and engaging in operations in Xikang. (November 2nd)

The Completion of the Lankao Closure Project is Imminent - Liu Zhi, Zhang Fang, and Others Inspect

Kaifeng dispatch: This year's Yellow River flood caused severe damage to Henan Province. Now that the period of high water has passed, various places are engaging in remedial work. The First Engineering Office of the Yellow River Conservancy Commission began construction on the 17th of last month to close the breaches in Lankao and Kaocheng counties. It borrowed the Ministry of Communications' radio station located at the Bian Telegraph Bureau to communicate with the breach closure sites on a daily basis. This morning (1st) at approximately 8:00 AM, Liu Zhi, Zhang Fang, Chen Ruzhen, two engineers from the Flood Relief Committee, Song Ke, provincial government technician Long Qingzhong, and adjutants and guards traveled by car to the two counties to survey the river project. At approximately 9:00 AM, they arrived in Lankao and rested briefly before being led by the county magistrate to inspect the breach at Xiaoxin Embankment north of Cailou Township. The foundation of the dike has been mostly completed, and there are currently over a thousand workers rushing to construct the remaining projects. At 11:30 AM, they arrived in Kaocheng. The county government office had been submerged by the flood, with collapsed walls and no rebuilding yet. The entire city remains a scene of devastation. At 12:00 PM, they arrived at the breach northeast of Yuanzhai. The dike foundation has been built three to four feet high, and there are over five hundred workers diligently working. At approximately 5:00 PM in the afternoon, they returned to Bian. The closure work is not difficult to complete. However, disaster relief for the affected people is a very major issue. At yesterday's regular meeting of the Provincial Relief Committee, it was reported that the Municipal Public Security Bureau stated that this year's Yellow River overflow caused an exceptionally severe flood, and refugees from the surrounding affected counties were continuously arriving in Bian to seek food, crying from hunger and cold. It was requested that the number of refugees in Bian be investigated and a list compiled for consideration and relief. It was decided to purchase 200 yuan worth of rice and distribute rice tickets to households in conjunction with the Public Security Bureau to provide relief. This one incident gives a glimpse of the entire situation. (November 1st)

Fierce Fighting Between Wang and You's Troops in Guizhou Province: You Guocai Attacks Guiyang in Two Routes; Over a Thousand Casualties in the Battle of Zhenyuan

Guangzhou dispatch: Since the dispute between Wang Jialie and You Guocai in Guizhou Province, their power has waxed and waned, and military conflict has continued unabated. Recently, Wang Jialie has been in power, forging alliances with neighboring provinces to solidify his position and continuously purchasing military equipment to expand the strength of his troops, strictly guarding against the resurgence of You Guocai and Mao Guangxiang. However, You and Mao were unwilling to remain dormant. After retreating into Sichuan, Mao Guangxiang raised funds and recruited soldiers on the Sichuan border, gaining considerable influence. After retreating to Xingren Panjiang, You has controlled the eight counties of Panjiang and recently advanced to occupy Shui Luodian, Ziyun, Guangshun, Dingfan, and Datang, appointing his own county magistrates, intercepting taxes, and increasing his troop strength to over 10,000 men. He has also joined forces with Mao Guangxiang's troops on the Sichuan border and Xi Woji's old troops on the Hunan border. Recently, he has declared war on Wang Jialie's troops. You's forces attacked Guiyang from two routes, with You personally leading the troops of Wan Baobang and others as the West Route Army and Che Mingyi, Lei Mingjiu, and Yang Qichang's three troops as the East Route Army. They launched simultaneous attacks on October 16th. Wang Jialie sent Liao Huaizhong, Wang Tianxi, and other troops to respond and telegraphed He Zhizhong, the commander of the First Division, urging him to return to Guiyang as soon as possible to discuss military strategy. It is reported that the two sides have been engaged in fierce fighting for days, especially in Zhenyuan and other places on the East Route, with over a thousand casualties on both sides. The outcome is still undecided. Both sides have backers in this conflict and have appealed to the provinces and regions they have previously contacted for assistance. As such, the civil war in Guizhou Province will likely not be resolved in a short time. (October 28th)

Songjiang

The Bizarre Assassination of a Cook

Chen Yonggen, the cook of the Public Records Rice Shop in this city, had previously guaranteed a certain amount of rice payments for Ayou, the cook of the Songjiang Grand Theatre. On the third day, he went to Ayou to collect 15 yuan and was returning home when, while passing the Gu Shui Daoyuan East of Zhu Xing Caishen Lane, he was suddenly attacked by thugs who stabbed him with sharp knives, causing serious injuries to his arms, face, and other areas. However, as it was around 7:00 PM and already dark, he could not identify the attackers. Later, he was informed by his friend, Zong Fugen, who lived nearby, who rushed him to Deqiong Hospital for treatment. His life is not in danger. The reason for the assassination is the subject of various rumors, and the money in his pocket was still there, suggesting that it was not a robbery. It may have been a love affair gone wrong.

Suzhou

Commissioner Gu of the Civil Affairs Department Inspects Suzhou

Gu Renfa, the Commissioner of the Jiangsu Civil Affairs Department, in order to inspect the administration of Suzhou and Changshu counties and to prepare for its reorganization, quietly left the provincial capital on the 3rd, after the routine meeting of the provincial government. He was accompanied by Secretary Yang Yiru. He arrived in Wuxi on the same day for an inspection. Yesterday (the 4th) afternoon, he arrived in Suzhou and first rested at the Garden Hotel. To avoid attracting attention, he used the pseudonym Wang Tongxuan and falsely claimed to be a member of the gentry. He then inspected the areas inside and outside the city for a week. His actions were very secretive, and at first, no one knew. Later, at 2:00 PM, he went to the Public Security Bureau, summoned the bureau chief and section chiefs for questioning and instruction. At 3:30 PM, he went to the county government to inspect for an hour. Before leaving, he gave instructions to the county magistrate and section chiefs. When reporters asked Gu for his opinions after inspecting Wuxian County, he replied with three points: (1) Autonomy: Wuxian County currently has thirteen autonomous districts, which is too many. In the future, they must be reduced and consolidated. According to regulations, each county should have fifteen districts. After consolidation, the funding and district administration should be better. (2) Public Security: It is heard that Wuxian County is rife with opium, gambling, and prostitution. The Public Security Bureau must work hard to investigate and ban them. If red pills manufacturing facilities are found, they should be handed over to military law for handling. However, the Commissioner himself (Gu Renfa referring to himself) once spent five jiao in Wuxi to buy twenty red pills, and after coming to Suzhou, he also spent one yuan to buy twenty pills, etc.

(3) Local Militia: In the future, military personnel must be appointed as deputy heads of the local militia. At 5:00 PM, he left the county government and planned to return to Zhenjiang that evening.

Wuxi

Second Installment of Land Value Tax Collection Begins

Zhao Dihua, the Commissioner of the Jiangsu Provincial Department of Finance, recently sent special commissioners to various counties to supervise and urge the payment of overdue taxes and grain tribute due to the serious shortage of funds in the treasury. Regarding the second installment of this year's land value tax, which in previous years was collected at the end of the solar calendar year, it is now proposed to change the previous method, extending the overdue period from February to March, and advancing it by one month, setting the collection to begin on November 14th. The tax rate is 5 jiao, 7 fen, 9 li, 6 hao per mu. To consider the livelihood of the people, the exemption of the previous year's additional grain tribute of 2 yuan per shi and the land survey fee of 1 jiao per mu is approved. Instructions were issued to all counties to comply. After receiving the order, the county government of this county immediately ordered the General Affairs Section to rush to print the blank forms and instructed the secretaries of each district to expedite the preparation of the tax rolls, requiring them to be completed and submitted to the county within three days for review and issuance of the blank rolls.

Government-Business Jointly Run Morning Granary Loans

County Magistrate Yan Shenyu, in order to pay attention to the rural economy, plans to cooperate with the pawnshop industry, inviting each township pawnshop to serve as an agent warehouse, providing low-interest capital, and handling the pawning of rice and grains. The industry believes that this matter is also beneficial to the country and convenient for the people, and should be vigorously assisted. Therefore, yesterday afternoon, a temporary meeting was convened at the Pawnshop Association on Lianyuan Street. The "Wuxi County Twenty-Second Year Rural Granary Loan Plan Draft" was discussed and resolved as follows: 1. Establish the Wuxi County Agricultural Granary Loan General Office, located in the Farmers Bank, with one representative each from the county government, the Farmers Bank, and the Agricultural Association as members, and designate the Farmers Bank representative as the director. 2. Each pawnshop in the rural area will be an agent agricultural granary, all under the control of the General Office. The interest rate is 1 fen and 6 li per month, uniformly. 3. In addition to the Farmers Bank's agricultural granary expanding the pledged rice and grain to 40,000 shi this year, the remaining rural pawnshop agent agricultural granaries will borrow a total of 200,000 yuan from various banks in Wuxi with the guarantee of the county government, the Farmers Bank, and the Pawnshop Association. The interest rate is 7 li, and the Farmers Bank and the Pawnshop Association will be responsible for distributing it appropriately based on the circumstances.

Citywide Street Vendors' Mass Petition

The county government of this county, in order to rectify the city appearance and maintain road traffic, specially instructed each sub-bureau chief to personally lead the police to earnestly persuade and ban fixed stalls that occupy sidewalks and build sheds in their respective jurisdictions, requiring them to be dismantled and moved voluntarily by November 10th. After receiving the instructions, the second sub-bureau chief Fan Xinzhi and the fifth sub-bureau chief Peng Xiwu respectively ordered the police to strictly ban the Tongyun Road, Hanchang Road, North Hanging Bridge, Daqiao Street, and North Tang Street areas in each jurisdiction, and took the stallholders Lu Wenbin, Yu Zixiang, and Tong Jingen to the bureau separately, ordering them to move. The stallholders were greatly alarmed upon hearing the news, so they gathered more than a hundred colleagues and sent two representatives on the previous day (the 3rd), leading the stallholders to the county government to petition, requesting consideration of the livelihood of ordinary people, providing relief, and approving exemption from the ban. As a result, they returned without success. Yesterday (the 4th), each stallholder gathered again two or three hundred vendors from all over the city, drafted a petition, and went to the county party headquarters to petition, but also did not get good results.

Nanhui

Bandit Leader Mao Muxiang Arrested in Jushan

The area around the outer Tangjiao corner of Nicheng, which belongs to this county, has always been a place where pirates appear. A well-known bandit leader named Mao Muxiang has formed gangs and roamed rampant for years, committing numerous crimes. The people in the area feared him like a tiger. Since County Magistrate Yuan took office, he has paid special attention to bandits along the coast. In April of this year, when County Magistrate Yuan personally went to Nicheng to search for bandit dens, Mao Muxiang had already fled far away, so he was not captured. Since then, many of his accomplices have been captured one after another. However, since Mao Muxiang fled, he has continued to roam the seas, pursuing his pirate career. At the end of last month, the bandit was selling stolen rice in the Jushan area of Dinghai County, Zhejiang Province, when he was encountered by Xiang Yuansheng and Yang Shulou, informants from this county. They secretly reported to the local water police team, which dispatched Inspector Wu Dongchen with several plainclothes policemen to arrest the bandit. At the same time, the informants reported to the county government of this county, which sent Detective Chief Zhu Zishen of the water patrol team with four policemen on the previous day (the 30th), carrying official documents and passports to Jushan to escort the bandit. However, the bandit had already been transferred by the local water police team to the Second Brigade of the Zhejiang Maritime Police. After Detective Chief Zhu tried every means, he finally brought him back yesterday (the 2nd). It is heard that the county government will severely punish him to pacify the area.

Changshu

Zheng Hongnian Visits Changshu

Zheng Hongnian, the Vice Minister of Transportation and President of National Jinan University, came to Changshu for sightseeing at the invitation of Ge Renyuan, the current Director of the Changshu Education Bureau. The Education Bureau prepared everything to welcome him, and slogans welcoming Zheng were hung along the way. The ship arrived at the port at 8:00 PM on the 3rd. County Magistrate Zhou Heng, Public Security Bureau Chief Yin Cunfu, and all staff members of the Education Bureau went to the wharf to greet him. Later, Zheng went to Suzhou due to business, and only his secretary Yang Zeheng, Hong Chen, Cui Tongjun, and more than eighty professors and students came. Director Ge, because of his friendship with the teachers and students, hosted a banquet at Hongyun Lou that night. Zheng returned to Changshu from Suzhou at 11:00 AM on the 4th. It is scheduled to give a lecture at Xiaoyao You today (the 5th) and visit various schools and social education institutions, and then visit Yushan. He will stay for about two days and then return to Shanghai.

Planning to Establish a Lvsi Fishery Special Zone

Lvsi is a famous fishing ground on the coast of the Yellow Sea. The Ministry of Industry plans to establish a fishery special zone. The Provincial Government believes that Jiangsu's important fishing areas and reclamation special zones are all in Jiangbei, which is an interdependent situation. The economic decline of rural and fishing villages is also the same. The relationship between them is very close, and the revitalization plan should take into account both. Therefore, County Magistrate Cheng was ordered to investigate and report the situation of the coastal fishing villages to the Fishery Association, and to prepare a revitalization plan for review, so that the Ministry can plan the fishery area.

Bandits Attempt to Kidnap Township Chiefs at Zhenwu Temple

Gu Sanliang Township of Zhenwu Temple, which belongs to this county, is located on the shore of Luyang Lake, where bandit activity is frequent. Several bandit boats suddenly came a few days ago and went ashore to kidnap the two township chiefs, Wang Bo and Xu Guohuai, saying that they had been notified a few days ago, but why hadn't they handled it yet, etc. Fortunately, the two township chiefs had heard the news in advance and avoided them, and were not harmed. The local people are now quite alarmed.

Jiashan

Wang Liangcheng Family Theft Case Solved

The home of Wang Liangcheng, a wealthy man in this county (president of the Zhengyan Daily), was suddenly robbed at night a few days ago, with gold ornaments and silver dollars stolen, valued at 2,000 yuan. Afterwards, the incident was reported to the Local Militia and the County Public Security Bureau. Director Xu Yanwu, in addition to personally leading a police team to pursue the criminals and inspecting the Wang residence for a week, also ordered the land and water police to investigate together. Four suspects, including Yang A Da, were arrested and interrogated strictly, and clues were obtained that the stolen goods were hidden in a thatched house on Xiaoshadu Road in Shanghai. Director Xu received the report and immediately sent several detectives, accompanied by Yang A Da and others, to Shanghai to pursue the stolen goods.

Shangyu

Zhou Zhaotang Arrested and Sent to the County

Zhou Zhaotang of Lianghu, Yuxi, was previously accused by Zhao Bowei of the same town in February of this year to the Provincial Department and Zhao Cisheng, Commissioner of the Seventh Administrative Special Zone, of organizing a crowd to intercept the Yuncheng Lan Qiongshan Buddhist scriptures, stealing and selling Song Dynasty editions of the Great Buddhist Canon, and smoking opium. Subsequently, the Provincial Zone repeatedly ordered the County Government to strictly investigate and reply. Zhou got the news and fled far away. He was repeatedly arrested but not captured. Although the Buddhist scriptures have now been moved to the county by Chen Zhongliang and others, the fourth district chief, and handed over to the Antiquities Preservation Committee for temporary care, sorting, and counting, a letter has been sent to the Shanghai Song Dynasty Buddhist Canon Association to send personnel to Shangyu for appraisal. Two volumes are indeed genuine Song Dynasty editions, but the catalog is missing and cannot be checked, so the case remains unresolved. Zhou secretly returned home a few days ago and was discovered by Zhao Bowei, who had previously filed a supplementary complaint with the Seventh Administrative Special Zone and received instructions to urge the County Government to arrest him. Therefore, on the afternoon of the 1st, he went to the county to report. The County Government received the report and, that night, ordered the police to go to Liang with Zhao to arrest Zhou Zhaotang and escort him to the city. The result of the court hearing in the afternoon was that the opium smoking part was first sent to the Weisheng Hospital for medical examination and treatment. The stolen and sold Buddhist scriptures part will be re-examined at a later date.

Xiaoshan

Xixing Huabu Rice Shop Careless

Run Maoyu Ji Huabu Rice Shop in Cang Lane, Xixing, Xiaoshan, was suddenly careless around 4:00 on the 1st, and three houses and three thatched houses were burned. At that time, in addition to taking out official documents and account books, all the yarn, flowers, rice, cloth, and groceries were valued at more than 1,000 yuan, all were burned. Fortunately, there were many people in the town who tried their best to rescue, and the town's merchants were not affected.

Girl Commits Suicide Due to Marriage Issues

Sun Rengu, a girl from Fengxi Village, Xixiang, Xiaoshan, is of marriageable age. Since entering Hangzhou Girls' Middle School, she has been fascinated by Europeanization. A few years ago, her parents arranged for her to marry the son of the Shi family. The 3rd of this month was the wedding date. Unexpectedly, the girl disliked her husband's appearance, so she tried to escape a day earlier, but was monitored by her family. On the morning of the 2nd, she secretly drank a bowl of oil and closed the door to pretend to sleep. When her family noticed and opened the door at noon, she was already lying dead, and her life was gone.

Sun Ke Arrives in Shanghai Yesterday Morning and Visits Song and Li Separately to Discuss Important Matters - Sun Talks About Song Agreeing to Go to Beijing to Preside Over the Economic Committee - Luo Wengan's Resignation as Foreign Minister Not Fully Decided

Sun Ke, the President of the Legislative Yuan, arrived in Shanghai by overnight train from Beijing at 7:30 yesterday morning. He then visited Song Ziwen, a standing member of the National Economic Committee, and Li Shizeng, a member of the Central Committee, etc. It is said that Mr. Song will take office in Beijing to preside over the affairs of the Economic Committee after the handover of the Ministry of Finance is completed. The control committees for the silk industry, etc., are also waiting for Mr. Song to return to Beijing to plan. The details are as follows:

Visiting Song and Li Separately

After arriving in Shanghai, Mr. Sun drove to Mr. Song Ziwen's private residence on Qiqi Road at 9:30 yesterday morning to urge Mr. Song to go to Beijing as soon as possible to preside over the National Economic Committee. He left after talking for about half an hour and went to the World College on Fukaixin Road to meet with Li Shizeng, a member of the Central Committee. Soon, Cai Yuanpei, a member of the Central Committee, also arrived. They discussed for about an hour. It is heard that the three met to exchange personal opinions on the current situation.

Mr. Sun's Remarks

When Mr. Sun left the World College, reporters rushed forward to inquire. According to him, the visits to Mr. Song and Mr. Li were just ordinary conversations and had no political meaning. Now Mr. Song (Ziwen) has expressed his willingness to continue to be responsible for the position of Standing Committee of the Economic Committee. Once the handover of the Ministry of Finance is completed, he can go to Beijing to preside over everything soon. The reporter then asked about the convening period of the Economic Committee and the preparation of the control committees for the silk industry, food, and coal industry. He replied that the preparation of the control committees for the silk industry, etc., is waiting for Mr. Song to return to Beijing to preside over. Furthermore, the candidates for the chairmen of each committee are still being carefully selected, and the second standing meeting of the Economic Committee can be held after Mr. Song goes to Beijing.

Luo Resigns as Foreign Minister

When Mr. Sun talked about this, the reporter asked about the central financial problem. Sun said that the central finance has generally been resolved, but all the details can be asked to the new Minister of Finance, Kong Xiangxi. Finally, the reporter asked about the rumors that Luo Wengan would resign as Minister of Foreign Affairs after returning to Beijing and specialize in the Minister of Judicial Administration, and at the same time, it was said that Huang Fu, the chairman of the Pingzheng Rectification Association, would succeed as Minister of Foreign Affairs. How true is it? He said that Luo's resignation as Minister of Foreign Affairs and specializing in judicial administration will be decided after Luo returns to Beijing. As for the rumor that Huang will succeed as Minister of Foreign Affairs, he has not heard of it.

Li Will Go Abroad

According to Li Shizeng, because the annual meeting of the Geneva World Cultural Conference will be held at the end of next month, he is preparing to leave to attend. There is no definite date for departure yet. It is heard that Mr. Li will go to Beijing in a few days to discuss with Wang Jingwei, the President of the Executive Yuan, etc.

First Batch of American Wheat Shipped to Shanghai at the End of the Month

Entrusted to American Merchant Alfred

The Amount is About 8,000 Tons

My country's loan of American wheat is worth a total of 10 million US dollars, equivalent to about 35 million national currency. Calculated at the market price, it should be at least 500,000 tons or more. It has been unloaded at ports such as Portland and Seattle in North America. Recently, Consul Mei, who was stationed in Portland, has taken office and can handle the visa procedures. Therefore, the American wheat began to be shipped to China on the 1st of this month. The shipping rights are exclusively undertaken by the American merchant Alfred, and the entire shipment will require at least 80 ships. Therefore, Alfred will rent more American ships and ship them to China in batches.

Already Shipped

For the first batch of American wheat, this port received a telegram from the United States stating that it had begun to be loaded on ships in Portland, USA. Although the amount was not specified, it was at least about 8,000 tons. The wheat is shipped from the United States, across the Pacific Ocean, and directly to Shanghai. It does not stop at any places along the way. According to reliable news obtained by reporters yesterday, it should arrive by the end of the month. It will be shipped in succession afterwards, but not all of it will be unloaded in Shanghai, or it will be delivered to various places in Beijing and Hubei.

Preparing Warehouses

The Ministry of Finance has entrusted the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company to be responsible for the loading, unloading, stacking, and lighterage of the American wheat to Shanghai. Therefore, the Cotton and Wheat Management Office informed the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company yesterday to prepare the Pudong Hua Warehouse as a place to store the American wheat. The Bureau has already notified the Hua Warehouse Wharf to check it.

Tomorrow (the 6th) is the first day of the Anti-Bandit Campaign Propaganda Week. It has been designated as Propaganda Day for All Circles. It has been specifically set to hold the "Shanghai Anti-Bandit Campaign Propaganda Conference for All Circles" at 10:00 AM in the auditorium of the Shanghai Chamber of Commerce. There will be a grand occasion when all circles meet tomorrow.

Agency Staff Must Participate

The Shanghai Municipal Party Committee notified each agency in a letter: "Sir, now is the time when the government is launching a large-scale anti-bandit campaign to eradicate the root of the cause. The people in the rear in various places should enthusiastically publicize it and become the government's backing. This committee, together with the two bureaus of education and society in this city, has specifically set from the 6th to the 11th of this month to hold the Anti-Bandit Campaign Propaganda Week, and will convene a Propaganda Conference for All Circles at 10:00 AM on the 6th in the auditorium of the Shanghai Chamber of Commerce. Airplanes Distribute Colorful Slogans

The outline of this propaganda week stipulates that airplanes should distribute slogans. It is now heard that the Shanghai Municipal Party Committee has printed one million colorful art slogans and sent personnel to contact the Aviation Association to ask the Aviation Administration to send airplanes to Shanghai to distribute them at that time, so as to arouse the serious attention of the people of the city to the anti-bandit campaign.

Postal Items Stamped with Anti-Bandit Seals

The Shanghai Municipal Party Committee sent a letter to the Postal Administration yesterday: "Sir, this committee, together with the two bureaus of education and society in this city, will hold an Anti-Bandit Campaign Propaganda Week from the 6th to the 11th of this month, in order to attract the attention of all circles to the anti-bandit work. This special letter is sent to you, hoping that you will check it and affix anti-bandit slogan seals on all postal items every day for one week from the 6th to the 11th."

Slogans Posted in All Shops in the City

During this propaganda week, in addition to the colorful small slogans distributed by airplanes, tens of thousands of posting slogans were also printed and distributed to the First and Second Special District Citizens' Associations for distribution to shops on various roads. They were all posted on the glass windows starting tomorrow. At the same time, the Boy Scout Council will transfer orders to all boy scout groups in the city, and set off today to post them on various roads, so that the citizens can be shocked and jointly rise up to eradicate them in order to stabilize the country and society.

Distributing Disaster Victims on Both Sides of the Yellow River

The Chinese and Foreign Charity Association at No. 12 Renji Road in this port, in view of the fact that the breach of the Yellow River this time has caused the most tragic disaster to the people on both sides, in addition to sending personnel to conduct on-site investigations, now that the weather is getting colder and the disaster victims are in urgent need of clothing, has already sent a large truck of 10,000 new cotton clothes from the North Station of the Beijing-Shanghai Railway yesterday and transferred them to the Jinpu Railway to Jining, so that they can be distributed to the disaster areas. It is heard that the cotton clothes released by the association are all self-purchased cotton and cloth, and workers are hired to supervise the production. They are heavy and thick cotton, which is cold-proof and durable. Its actual benefits to the disaster victims are truly not shallow.

The China Foreign Famine Relief General Association Held Its First General Meeting of Sponsors Yesterday

A Very Enthusiastic Response to Donations on the Spot

The China Foreign Famine Relief General Association's Honorary Presidents Wang Zhengting and Zhu Qinglan, along with Chen Guangfu, Chairman of the Yangtze Advisory Committee, held the association's first general meeting of sponsors yesterday afternoon at the ninth floor of the Eight Immortals Bridge YMCA. More than thirty people attended, including Wang Zhengting, Chen Guangfu, Zhu Qinglan, Wu Yiting, Huang Hanzhi, Guan Jiongzhi, Wu Tiecheng (represented by Luo Panhui), Zhao Jinqing, Zhu Yinjiang, Lu Bohong, Xu Qianlin, and Westerners An Xianjin and Bei Gen. Wang Zhengting was publicly elected as chairman, and Shen Mingsan provided warm hospitality. Everyone took their seats for a meal, after which Wang Zhengting stood up to report, saying that this year's Yellow River flood has caused people in Henan, Shandong, and other provinces to be displaced, unable to farm their fields, and without clothing, food, or shelter. This year they cannot survive the winter, and next year is even more unimaginable. The government is extremely anxious. Now Mr. Chen Guangfu, based on his experience in relieving the victims of the Yangtze River disaster, has stepped forward to relieve the victims of the Yellow River disaster. However, the disaster is widespread and the funds are meager. It is hoped that the gentlemen present will donate money to save lives, so that the disaster victims may have hope of survival. Donation books were then distributed. Mr. An Xianjin then reported that more than 20,000 yuan had been donated by Westerners, and that more would be remitted in the future. Mr. Wu Zhihao first advanced 1,000 yuan. Mr. Wang Yiting, Huang Hanzhi, and Guan Jiongzhi, representing the Yellow River Emergency Relief Association, donated 2,000 yuan. Mr. Lu Bohong donated 1,000 yuan. After the report, there was a round of applause. The meeting adjourned after the meal, which was after 2 pm.

Telephone Bureau Notice Regarding Long-Distance Call Surcharge

Starting From the 15th of This Month

The Surcharge Will Be Changed to One Dime Per Call

The Shanghai Telephone Bureau of the Ministry of Communications issued a special notice yesterday regarding the special handling fee to be charged to recipients of long-distance calls. The notice stated: "Based on the letter forwarded by the Jiangsu Long-Distance Management Office, and the Instruction No. 5497 from the Ministry of Communications, regarding the special handling fee to be charged to recipients of long-distance calls, regardless of the province or region, starting from November 15 of this year, a flat surcharge of one dime will be charged to the caller for each call. The calling range is limited to within ten li of the recipient's location. Please take note and inform accordingly." In addition to separate notifications, this notice is hereby issued for public knowledge.
