The Jianghai Customs "Hexing" Cruiser Was Launched Yesterday　Mrs. Ployart, Wife of the Chief of the Customs Preventive Division, Threw the Bottle　Full Completion Expected by the End of January Next Year

The Jiangnan Shipyard of the Naval Department is building the Jianghai Customs' three cruisers, the "Dexing," "Lianxing," and "Hexing." The "Dexing" and "Lianxing" have already been launched. The "Hexing" was launched at 2 pm yesterday. Mrs. Ployart, wife of the Chief of the Customs Preventive Division, threw the bottle. The details are as follows:

Participants

The "Hexing" cruiser at the southern end of the No. 3 dock of the Gaochang Temple Shipyard had a temporary wooden platform built next to it. The platform was surrounded by ten thousand flags. The national flag and a champagne bottle wrapped in colored silk were hung at the bow of the ship. A platoon of soldiers from the naval guard battalion was specially dispatched to maintain strict security. Among those who attended the ceremony were Chen Zaofan, Deputy Director of the Jiangnan Shipyard of the Naval Department; Ren Guanghai, Staff Officer of the Training Fleet Headquarters, and his wife; Chief Engineer Mao Gen and his wife; Mrs. Ployart, wife of the Chief of the Customs Preventive Division, and her husband; and more than twenty captains of naval ships stationed in Shanghai, such as the "Xianning" and "Funing."

The Launching of the "Hexing" Cruiser (Photo Courtesy of the East China News Agency)

The Launching Ceremony

At 2 pm, Chen Zaofan, Deputy Director of the Jiangnan Shipyard, presided over the ceremony and reported, saying, "Today is the launching of the 'Hexing' cruiser. We are very honored to have everyone here. The 'Hexing' is the third of the largest cruisers of the Jianghai Customs. The 'Dexing' and 'Lianxing' have already been launched. Please invite Mrs. Ployart to perform the bottle-throwing ceremony." Then, Mrs. Ployart forcefully threw the champagne bottle on the bow of the ship. With a loud bang, champagne splashed everywhere, and the ship was launched amidst cheers. It was towed by a small tugboat to a stop next to the shipyard's dock.

Cruiser Structure

The "Hexing" cruiser is 170 feet long, 32 feet wide, 16 feet 6 inches deep, with a draft of 11 feet 6 inches, a displacement of 700 tons, a speed of 13 nautical miles per hour, and 160 horsepower. It is expected to be completed by the end of January next year. As for the "Dexing" and "Lianxing" cruisers, which were launched in September this year, they are expected to be completed by the end of this year.

Zhang Zhichao's Troops Seized Two Japanese Warships at Sanchahe　Killing Japanese and Puppet Troops Over Three Days and Capturing Two Captains Alive　The Rest Jumped into the River and Drowned, the Number Unknown　Japan and Russia Are Actively Preparing for War, Eruption Imminent

Zhang Zhichao, Commander-in-Chief of the East China National Salvation Army, specially dispatched Captain Wang Chuanjing, from the Daqingshan mountain area on the border of Heilongjiang, to send a letter to his representative in Shanghai, Zhang Zhendong, reporting that his troops had seized the Japanese traitorous warships "Yinxiang" and "Daheihe" on the night of the ninth of last month at Sanchahe. A reporter from the Far East News Agency met with Representative Zhang yesterday, who kindly introduced him to Mr. Wang. The details of the conversation are recorded below:

Disguised Arrival in Shanghai

I (Wang said himself) came to Shanghai this time upon the personal instructions of Commander-in-Chief Zhang Zhichao to meet Representative Zhang and report on the recent military situation of our troops and the seizure of the two Japanese traitorous warships at Sanchahe. I departed from the Daqingshan base camp on the border of Heilongjiang on the 16th of last month, disguised as a camel cart driver, carrying sheepskin goods. Upon arriving at Bayan, I gifted the camel cart to the farmers. Carrying sheepskin goods, I took a boat to Harbin. The Japanese army there conducted unusually strict inspections, with a total of nine checkpoints. They thought I was a merchant, so they did not interrogate me severely. On the 23rd, I took a train from Harbin to Dalian. On the same day, I took a boat from Dalian and arrived in Shanghai yesterday morning. I don't know how many dangers I encountered along the way, but fortunately, I was able to turn danger into safety and arrive safely.

Warship Seizure Circumstances

A few months ago, there was a popular uprising in several counties in western Heilongjiang. The cause was the excessive oppression of the people by the Japanese. Unable to bear it any longer, they rose up. After the uprising, the people formed armies to resist the Japanese. However, the incident grew larger and larger. The Japanese Kwantung Army stationed in Harbin received the report and immediately dispatched three battalions of marines and three warships to suppress the uprising. When the "Yinxiang" and "Daheihe" warships sailed up the Nenjiang River to Sanchahe, our troops were already prepared and seized them. The details are in Commander-in-Chief Zhang's letter to Representative Zhang, so I won't repeat them. (To be continued)

Japan and Russia Prepare for War

Recently, both Japan and Russia are in a state of high tension, with the situation being very serious, and an immediate outbreak is imminent. Both sides have completed the important wartime work. The Japanese-held combat areas are: one at Suifenhe Five Stations, one at Heihe, and one at Manzhouli. These three places are the gateways for the Japanese, and they are heavily guarded, with three or four divisions stationed at each place. Five layers of trenches have been built, connecting to various locations, and can accommodate heavy trucks. The artillery emplacements are made of reinforced steel and concrete. The Russian-held areas are: Boli, Hunchun River, the north bank of the Heilongjiang River, Hailanpao, the east bank of the Ussuri River, Shuangchengzi, and other places. The defense work is extremely meticulous and thorough. The construction of the airfield is also very solid and good. At present, both sides are eager to try. According to my observation, the outbreak is only a matter of time. The Japanese are training puppet troops to be driven forward, which is especially heartbreaking. However, the sinister intentions of the Japanese are evident from this.

Zhang Zhichao's Letter

Zhendong, my brother, I hope this letter finds you well. I trust that the letter sent previously by Zhou Fu, as well as the letter to Brother Du Yuesheng, have reached you. A few months ago, a popular uprising occurred in several counties in the west due to the oppression by the Japanese. The people were forced to form volunteer armies to resist them. Because the momentum was great, the Japanese army heard the news and urgently reported it to the Kwantung Army stationed in Harbin. The army, upon receiving the urgent report, immediately dispatched three battalions of marines on the 8th from Harbin aboard the "Yinxiang" and "Daheihe" warships along the Songhua River to the Nenjiang River, intending to fight against the volunteer army formed by the popular uprising. We learned of this in advance, and then on both banks of the Sanchahe, the border between Nenjiang and Songhua, we hurriedly dug more than two hundred trenches, preparing to fight to the death with the Japanese army. On the evening of the 9th, the two Japanese warships sailed to Sanchahe. The banks were covered with willows, and the river was narrow. The Japanese army was not familiar with the navigation route and immediately dropped anchor. The Japanese army did not know that volunteer soldiers were ambushed on both banks. At around 11 o'clock that evening, it rained lightly, and it was exceptionally dark. Then, more than one hundred volunteer soldiers secretly sailed close to the Japanese warships on four wind boats and issued a secret order. They leaped onto the two Japanese warships, and gunfire erupted from all sides. The Japanese army was completely unprepared and soundly asleep. The two sides then engaged in hand-to-hand combat on the ship for about three hours, killing more than three hundred Japanese and puppet soldiers and capturing two Japanese captains alive. The rest jumped into the river and drowned, and the number of deaths is unknown. In this battle, the "Yinxiang" and "Daheihe" warships, 171 rifles, 4 pistols, 4 machine guns, 4 cannons, and 2 anti-aircraft guns were seized. More than sixty Japanese soldiers were injured on the ships. There was another ship following the two warships, but its name is unknown. After hearing the gunfire, the ship sounded an emergency siren and quickly fled. Sincerely, your brother Zhichao, October 15th night at the base camp.

The Production and Sales Company's Letter to the Industrial Sector: National Strength Should Be Cultivated Before the War　People Should Assist the Government in Striving for Production　Fifth Preparatory Committee Meeting Held Yesterday

Since the Preparatory Office of the China National Products Production and Sales Joint Company issued its first announcement, various provinces have responded enthusiastically. There has been an especially eager response in sending letters and telegrams to participate in the founding and pay share funds. In order to facilitate the payment of shares by various provinces, the Preparatory Office convened its fifth preparatory committee meeting yesterday. Wang Xiaolai presided over the meeting, and Wu Zhihao reported on the recent progress and discussed the draft proposals for branch companies, national products warehouses, and chain stores. Finally, in addition to resolving to send a letter to the General Administration of the Bank of China, requesting the General Administration of the Bank of China to notify its branch offices in various locations to collect share funds on its behalf, it was also resolved to issue a letter to the national industrial sector. The wording is alert and thought-provoking, and it is expected that the industrial sector will rise up in response. The original text is recorded below so that the industrial sector across the country, which is working hard on production, can form a self-help and mutual aid association.

The Preparatory Office of the China National Products Production and Sales Joint Company's Respectful Letter to the National Industrial Sector: All those who are concerned about the national crisis are focusing on the world's future war as the current major issue facing our country. Once a great war breaks out, will we help A to attack B, or will we help B to attack A? Or will we allow A and B to commit suicide, and we will not take sides, standing far outside the circle of war to protect ourselves? Or will we wait for A and B to become exhausted, and then we will rise up as Bian Zhuang? This is not only a policy that the government should decide which is more beneficial, but all of our people should also prepare for how to assist the government. There must be preparations before there is strength, and only with strength can the people's opinions be valued by the government. Therefore, striving for production and cultivating national strength are the most important tasks that the people must not delay today. On the day of the company's announcement of the solicitation of shares, my colleagues could not help but offer our most sincere, albeit meager, insights to the industrial sector across the country, which is striving for production. The national strength of a country is entirely entrusted to the economy, and the principles of the economy are entirely based on land and people. My colleagues have already said this. From what we have said, it can be seen that the industrial sector, which is striving for production today, should know the importance of its position and carefully plan the strategies for struggling for production and for the country. Here, my colleagues would like to ask the industrial sector: Is the establishment of factories that our country needs today fully prepared, and there is no room for increase? Has the productivity of existing factories reached its limit and there is no room for increase? Is the production volume of existing factories equal to the national demand, and there is no room for increase? Are there already facts of oversupply of products produced by existing factories, and there is no way to promote them? Everyone knows that this is not the case. In view of the quantity of imported foreign goods, the reports of a sharp increase in enemy goods, and the fact that the people are forced to buy them out of need, knowing that this is like drinking poison to quench thirst, it can be seen that there are countless factories that urgently need to be built, and existing factories need to be expanded, and there are products that need to be sold. This is enough to prove that the path for the industrial sector to struggle for its own production and for the country is still extremely broad. However, with such a broad path, why does the industrial sector abandon itself and not strive for it? The answer is that it is not that the industrial sector does not want to strive, but that it is trapped by financial resources, lacks talent, or is hindered by the mutual slaughter of competition, and is unable to do anything. Therefore, the industrial sector, which is enthusiastic about production, must work together to create a new path for self-help, otherwise it is not enough to talk about production, nor is it enough to talk about struggling for the country. And the fall of the Northeast, the crisis in North China, or even the areas that have not fallen or are not in danger, are successively being controlled by the power of the violent enemy, and the facts of falling into danger are continuously emerging, or even more unfortunately, the whole country falls into destruction. Then, the description of the future world history, I am afraid that the arrows of blame will not all be collected on the government, but will be collected on our people. This is also why the industrial sector, which is striving for production today, in order to avoid future generations' blame, and in order to prevent future generations from becoming slaves, must recognize the new path of self-help and jointly strive for production and for the country. This is what my colleagues want to announce to the national industrial sector with the plan to establish the China National Products Production and Sales Joint Company. We sincerely hope that the national industrial sector will take the belief of self-help and mutual assistance and jointly assist in participating. The target of participation does not seek a large amount of investment, but only hopes that with the smallest investment, my colleagues can have a chance to do their best to plan. The sequential implementation of the plan in the future is to gradually complete the new path required by the production sector, which is striving for production. This new path is to call on enthusiastic people to organize local branch companies and establish chain stores to set up a sales network. The second is to unite the financial sector, organize national products warehouses, and undertake the flow of national products. The third is to gather specialized talents, organize research institutions, and establish industrial schools to create a pool of ideas and talent cultivation. All three of these are urgently needed by our industrial sector and are sufficient to help achieve the aspirations of various provinces to struggle for their own production and for the country. Moreover, the development of production and the increase of national strength are undoubtedly guaranteed. Even when the great war comes in the future, it can assist the government in deciding on the choice of policies. There is absolutely no justice or right or wrong in the world. If you want to clarify right and wrong, you must rely on strength. You must rely on strength to be able to cope with the advantages and disadvantages of the war. Otherwise, people will be knives and chopping boards, and we will be fish and meat. Even if the national disaster does not lead to immediate destruction, it will inevitably become a dependent, subservient state. May I ask the people of the country, are they willing to be the people of a dependent state? Now, the leaders of the party-state and the governors of various provinces are enthusiastically optimistic about the implementation of the plan and are rising up to assist based on the principle of common cooperation between the government and the people. Some send jointly signed founding certificates, while others send enthusiastic letters of support. The unity of the government and the public has laid the foundation. Do not miss the opportunity to dedicate yourself to saving the country. The benefits and methods of participation are hereby announced as follows. It is hoped that the industrial sector across the country, which is striving for production, will take note.

Zhu Jiqing's Mission to the South　Preparing to Announce Income and Expenditure of Donations

Zhu Jiqing, member of the Central Executive Committee, has been living in seclusion in Beiping since returning from the Northeast to fight against Japan. Previously, because Mr. Wang Leping's coffin was buried at Thousand Buddha Mountain in Jinan, Mr. Zhu made a special trip from Peiping to Jinan to participate in the main sacrifice and other matters. He then went to Qingdao to tour Laoshan, Boshan, Taishan, and the Confucius Temple. He arrived in Nanjing on October 31. Mr. Zhu told visitors yesterday that this trip to Nanjing was firstly to attend the public sacrifice for Mr. Wang Leping in Jinan, and secondly to sort out the income and expenditure accounts of the anti-Japanese army that he commanded in the past two years. The estimated total amount of donations received was 336,874.58 yuan (previously published in the Shanghai Shenxin and other newspapers). The total expenditure for military equipment, salaries, and other expenses for this anti-Japanese war was 354,226.617 yuan, including: military supplies and clothing: 13,738.74 yuan; supplies and relief: 68,625.986 yuan; military activity expenses: 107,974.731 yuan; transportation and travel expenses: 29,875.28 yuan; miscellaneous expenses: 30,090.599 yuan; postal and telecommunications: 6,374.28 yuan; purchase of military equipment: 66,050.432 yuan; medical and relief expenses: 2,512.23 yuan; office expenses: 11,161.563 yuan; food expenses: 17,822.857 yuan. The total amount of expenses exceeded the income by more than 17,000 yuan. This amount of more than 17,000 yuan can only be treated as the foreign debt of the anti-Japanese army, which will be repaid in the future. After the above income and expenditure figures are submitted to the Economic Committee of our army for review, they will be printed into a booklet and distributed to various donating organizations or individuals and various groups. It is currently being rushed to completion, and it will probably be announced to the public soon, he said.

Dredging of the South Waterway of the Huangpu River　Traffic Prohibited　Shipping Companies Must Pay Attention

The Port Director of the Jianghai Customs, Valeryen, believes that the waterway in the southern area of the Huangpu River is becoming increasingly silted up, which hinders navigation. Therefore, dredging began yesterday. In order to make shipping companies pay attention, he issued Notice No. 21, stating: "Regarding the scheduled dredging of sections 7, 8, and 9 of the Huangpu River, Notice No. 18 was issued on October 25 of this year to inform the public. It is now scheduled to start dredging the aforementioned locations on the 4th of this month. Traffic is prohibited in the south waterway, namely the Pudong waterway, from that date until the date of completion of the project is announced separately. All shipping companies must take note. This notice is hereby issued."

Two Ocean Liners Survive a Hurricane

(Haishun) The Haishun Wheel of the Haichang Company set off from Xiamen to Shanghai on the 23rd of last month. On the way, it suddenly encountered a hurricane. For the sake of safe navigation, the ship specifically took shelter from the wind in Huidao, off the coast of Xiamen, to avoid danger. After a week of hardships along the way, it finally entered the port safely yesterday. It is scheduled to sail to Yingkou today.

(Longshan) The China Merchants Steam Navigation Company rented the Longshan of Sanbei. On November 1, the ship reached the Dacha Mountain sea area while sailing to Qingdao. Suddenly, it encountered a hurricane, and the ship's captain immediately took shelter in the strait to avoid being hit. After the wind passed, it arrived in Qingdao without damage, but it was delayed. According to people in the shipping industry, this hurricane was the last one of this year.

United States Far East Trade Statistics for August

Continental News reported yesterday (3rd) that it received a message from the US Department of Commerce that the US's total imports and exports for Far East trade in August was valued at 64,194,000 yuan, (US dollars below as well) less than the 71,720,000 yuan for the last month by 7,526,000 yuan. This was mostly due to decreased US exports of cotton to the Far East and sugar from the Philippines to the US. However, compared to the same period last year, valued at 40,171,000 yuan, this has increased by 22,023,000 yuan. Excluding the Philippines, US imports from the Far East all increased significantly, and US exports to the Far East decreased only slightly to China, Siam, and Vietnam compared to last August. It was learned that the US purchases of goods from China in August this year totaled 5,478,000 yuan, almost doubling compared to the same period last year. US purchases of goods from Japan also increased by 40 percent, with silk fabrics, camphor, and crab meat showing the largest increases. As for Chinese goods, it seems that they generally increased and there was nothing special. Furthermore, among the US exports sold to China, except for tobacco, cedar, automobiles, and aircraft equipment, which slightly increased, the rest were not much different from last year. The total value decreased from 4,815,000 yuan to 4,704,000 yuan, a decrease of about 2 percent.

Huang Yuzhai Exerts Efforts to Mediate the Rent Dispute in Xiang'anfang, Zhabei; Landlord and Tenants' Negotiations Break Down; Mr. Huang Acts as Mediator, Dispute Resolved

The houses in Xiang'anfang, Chang'an Road, Zhabei, are managed by the Rongchang Real Estate Department. A month ago, the tenants in the neighborhood, due to the disparity in rents, demanded rent reductions from the landlord, leading to a dispute between the two parties. Both sides took extreme positions and refused to yield. The landlord argued that due to cost factors, they could not make a profit and therefore could not reduce the rent. On the other hand, the tenants insisted on a reduction due to the commercial downturn. Negotiations broke down, with neither side willing to compromise. The landlord even reported tenant Wang Jianming for organizing an illegal group. Although the Social Bureau and the Public Security Bureau intervened for mediation, the results were ineffective. Both sides filed petitions, seeking legal remedies, inevitably leading to a lawsuit in court. Now, Mr. Huang Yuzhai has stepped in to mediate, exerting his best efforts to resolve the situation. After repeated consultations and clarifying that the matter involving Wang Jianming was a misunderstanding, both sides, feeling Mr. Huang's dedicated efforts to overcome the difficulties and resolve the dispute, agreed to compromise. The landlord voluntarily reduced the rent for one and a half months and was responsible for repairing the houses and installing electric lights. Thus, this dispute came to an end. Without Mr. Huang's assumption of the difficult task and his best efforts to mediate, this major dispute would have been unimaginable. It is now heard that both the landlord and the tenants have voluntarily published statements in the newspaper, expressing their satisfaction.

Carpenter Chops Young Woman After Plotting to Renew Old Affair Fails

A local woman, Ms. Chen, lives at No. 9, Hongfu Lane, Xinzha Road. Her husband, Chen Azhu, works as a cook. However, Ms. Chen was formerly intimate with a carpenter named Jin Fa. After marrying Chen Azhu, the two cut off contact. Unexpectedly, yesterday morning around 9:00 AM, while Chen Azhu was out at work, the carpenter Jin Fa suddenly went to Ms. Chen's house, intending to talk to her and hoping to rekindle their old affair. However, Ms. Chen refused and told him to leave. This caused a conflict between them, and Jin Fa, unable to contain his anger, took out a working axe that he had been carrying and chopped at Ms. Chen. Fortunately, Ms. Chen dodged quickly and was only grazed by the axe on her left temple. She immediately screamed for help. Seeing that things were not going well, Jin Fa quickly fled. Neighbors, hearing the commotion, reported the incident to the Xinzha police station, which dispatched a vehicle to send Ms. Chen to Baolong Hospital for treatment. As the injury was minor, she was bandaged by the doctor and left the hospital on her own to report the incident to the police station. The police dispatched detectives to arrest the suspect, but he had already fled. The police have redeployed officers to secretly arrest him.

Pang Fengzhi and Others Accused of Fraud

Pang Fengzhi, manager of the Huadong Bank on Ningbo Road, who is from Wuxing, and Sun Zhizhai have recently been accused of fraud by Li Dehua, a resident of No. 32, Xiafei Lane, Xiafei Road in the French Concession, who runs an import and export business and is from Pinghu. Lin Xianjian and Young Woman Jia Lin's Marriage Dispute Case: Doubts Arise Regarding Lin's Evidence

Wu Bin (courtesy name Chuba), a staff member of the First Section of the Jiangsu Provincial Government, married Ms. Jia Lin (courtesy name Huixian), an acquaintance from the past, as his second wife in Nanjing on July 30 of this year through a matchmaker. Before Jia and Wu were married, Jia was intimate with Lin Xianjian, the director of the Xianjian Hospital on Jiangxi Road, who is from Jieyang, Guangdong. Because Lin never agreed to marry her, she left Lin on July 24. After marrying Wu, she wanted to retrieve her belongings left with Lin, so she accompanied Wu to Shanghai to get them. Lin immediately reported the incident to the police station, claiming that Jia was his legal wife and had committed adultery with Wu. Based on his claims, the police filed a public prosecution against Wu and Jia. After repeated hearings in the First Special District Court, the defendant Jia Lin not only recounted the beginning of her seduction by Lin Xianjian during the Shanghai war last spring through cunning means but also pointed out that the marriage certificate and her wedding photo presented by Lin were altered or forged, requesting an investigation. The court granted her request and postponed the case to send official letters to the Jieyang County Government and government offices in Hangzhou and other places. During this time, Wu Bin separately filed a criminal self-accusation against Lin Xianjian for forging evidence and slander. That case has already been tried, and the defendant Lin Xianjian was sentenced to two months of imprisonment, with probation granted. The public prosecution of adultery is now being handled because the replies from various government offices have been arriving in Shanghai one after another. This morning, Presiding Judge Feng Shide continued the hearing. Before the hearing, the plaintiff and defendant were conducting a reconciliation in the courthouse's waiting room. The negotiations between the two sides were very close, and a peaceful resolution seemed possible. However, as the case was a public prosecution, it could not be freely dismissed. When the hearing opened, both parties still appeared in court to be questioned. Presiding Judge Feng first announced the replies from various places, and based on what was said in the documents, it was proven that Lin Xianjian's statements were mostly false. However, Lin still tried to justify himself with sophistry. The court, seeing that the facts of the case were already clear, ordered the beginning of the debate. The police lawyer, Ru Baoyi, immediately stated that although the plaintiff had presented various pieces of evidence, they not only failed to prove that he and Jia Lin were formally married, but the evidence itself was questionable and therefore should not be believed. He requested that the defendants be declared not guilty. Presiding Judge Feng then announced that a date would be set for the verdict.

Carriage Wheel Breaks, Bride Bleeds

Si Bao, the daughter of rice merchant Wu Qiaosheng, married Lu Heshang, the owner of a cigarette and paper shop in Jiangwan, last month through a matchmaker. The day before yesterday was the new bride's full-month celebration. Heshang returned to his father-in-law's house with his wife. They hired a carriage and prepared several kinds of gifts. The carriage was old and dilapidated. As they were traveling along Xietu Road, dozens of steps away from Wu's house, the wheel disc of the carriage suddenly broke, causing the carriage to overturn. Heshang and his wife both hit their heads and faces on the glass window, breaking it and causing them to bleed profusely. The coachman also fell down. The coachman managed to drag Lu Heshang and his wife out of the carriage. The bride's hands and clothes were stained with blood. Wu, after being informed, rushed over and took his daughter and son-in-law to his house, where he washed the blood off their faces and gave them clothes to change into. The bride suffered minor injuries and was frightened. Wu is now keeping his daughter and son-in-law at his house.

Young Woman Hangs Herself

Madam Pan Chen, from Changzhou, was 30 years old and married to Pan Manshan, who is now 31 years old and works as an engraver, earning only 15 yuan a month. The couple lived in a small room upstairs at the Sishichun Noodle Shop on Zhaozhou Road in the South City. After they married, they were initially harmonious. However, because Pan's monthly income was limited, their lives were quite difficult, and their family gradually became discordant. Quarrels often arose within the household. Yesterday evening at 7:30, the couple argued again over a trivial matter. Madam Chen, harboring thoughts of ending her life, took advantage of Pan's absence and hanged herself in the room. When Pan returned home after finishing his work, she had already died, but her body was not yet cold. He rushed her to Renji Hospital, but it was too late. Pan reported the incident to the Second District Headquarters, waiting for instructions to inform the local authorities and request an examination by the local court.

Russian Woman Sentenced to Death for Murdering Lover Yang Ge Appeals

The Shanghai Times reports that Mrs. Hatley, a Russian woman, who was accused of murdering her lover, Yang Ge, on August 16 of this year, was sentenced to death by Jones, the British Assessor in China, on October 18. She has since filed an appeal, and a full court hearing is scheduled to open in Shanghai on December 4. In addition to the original trial judge, the British Assessor, two more judges are needed. One will come to Shanghai from Hong Kong. How the court will be organized has not yet been announced. When the British Assessor delivered the verdict, the 12 jurors, while deciding that the woman was guilty, strongly requested clemency. The Assessor's verdict and the jurors' request have been submitted to the British Minister to China, and the execution must be approved by the British Minister. However, the British Minister also has the power to pardon, but a decision can only be made after the appellate court has made its final ruling. A petition signed by the British community in Shanghai to the British Minister for clemency will also be issued in the coming days.

Hubei Fellow-Provincials Association Dispute Resolved

Hubei natives residing in Shanghai, wishing to unite their fellow-provincials' sentiments, originally formed the Hubei Fellow-Provincials Association in Shanghai. Later, some members, dissatisfied with the association's organizers monopolizing association affairs, formed the All-Hubei Public Association and the Hubei Fellow-Provincials Association Preparatory Committee to counter the association. This led to frequent disputes among Hubei native organizations in Shanghai. All three parties petitioned the Party and government for a fair judgment. Several years passed without a resolution. Now, it is learned that the Municipal Party Department and the Social Bureau convened representatives from the three organizations yesterday to discuss the matter and establish three measures to resolve the issue. The attendees included Peng Yuncen, Hong Shiwei, and Yu Yanqing from the Hubei Fellow-Provincials Association in Shanghai; Liu Wanqing, Yao Jiapeng, and Zhang Chuqiang from the All-Hubei Public Association; and Zhu Dehe, Tao Zhengwu, and Wu Ziyou from the Hubei Fellow-Provincials Association Preparatory Committee. Cui Conghao of the Social Bureau presided over the meeting, with Zhang Xiaotong attending from the Municipal Party Department. The resolution measures are as follows: (1) The Hubei Fellow-Provincials Association in Shanghai, the All-Hubei Public Association, and the Hubei Fellow-Provincials Association Preparatory Committee will each nominate one representative, new members will nominate one representative, and Guan Jiongzhi, who is enthusiastic about public welfare, will be publicly nominated, for a total of five people to form the Standing Committee of the Hubei Fellow-Provincials Association in Shanghai to handle all association affairs. (2) The Standing Committee must be established before November 10, and Guan Jiongzhi will convene the meeting. (3) The procedures for members of the Hubei Fellow-Provincials Association Preparatory Committee and the All-Hubei Public Association to join the association will be handled by the Standing Committee in accordance with the law.

Siming Bank Inspection Report

The Siming Bank issued its reserve preparation inspection report for October 31, stating that the bank's banknotes issued were fully backed by reserves, with at least 60% in cash reserves and at most 40% in guarantee reserves. The inspection report by accountants Wu Zheng and Pan Zhaobang and supervisors Xiang Fenglou and Xu Boxiong is as follows: The total amount of exchange coupons issued is 17,690,800 yuan. The total amount of reserves is 17,690,800 yuan, including the bank's issued amount of 8,890,800 yuan, with cash reserves of 7,790,800 yuan and a guarantee of 1,100,000 yuan. Pushan Villa Charity Report

In October, Shanghai Pushan Villa collected and buried 82 large coffins, 2,012 small coffins, and 8 bone urns in both the Chinese and foreign-controlled areas. It gave out 864 large and small coffins, including 30 large coffins and 1,313 small coffins collected by the villa itself. The Xieqiao branch villa and various charitable halls in the French Concession collected 280 small coffins and 8 bone urns. In addition, the Public Concession police stations and hygiene departments collected a total of 40 large coffins and 419 small coffins of abandoned infant corpses and unclaimed corpses from various hospitals within the concession, according to their inquiries. The Red Cross hospitals collected 4 large coffins, the Shanghai Shipi Hospital collected 3 large coffins, the Tongren Hospital collected 4 large coffins, and the Huili Hospital collected 1 large coffin. All of the above corpses were collected by the villa's vehicles and transported to the charity cemetery for burial, marked for identification. In addition, the New Min Road White Cross Pushan Hospital provided free medical treatment and medicine to a total of 5,180 patients.

French Concession Vehicle Accident Cases in October

The French Concession Vehicle Affairs Office released statistics on vehicle accidents in the French Concession in October 1933. There were a total of 214 accidents, including two fatal cases, one on Rue Amiral Bayle and one on Avenue Foch. Twenty-one people were injured and sent to the hospital for treatment, 57 were sent to the hospital for dressing, and 8 were dressed at the police station. There were 22 bicycle accidents, with 7 pedestrians being knocked down. The following is a table showing the proportion of vehicle accidents in October 1932, September 1933, and October 1933.

| Number of all accidents | 214 | 182 | 191 |

Zhao Weixian Sues Wei Tingrong and His Son for Instigating False Accusation and Obstructing Freedom. The Second Special Court Opened the Hearing Yesterday, with a Large Crowd of Onlookers. Because the Police Lawyer Participated, the Judge Considered It Inappropriate. As a Result, the Hearing Could Not Proceed and Will Be Rescheduled.

Wei Tingrong, former commander-in-chief of the French Concession's Chinese Volunteer Corps and manager of the Zhongfa Silver Company, was the eldest son-in-law of the late Shanghai tycoon Zhu Baosan. On July 24 of the 18th year of the Republic of China (1929), at around 11:00 AM, Wei, accompanied by his two sons, was driving home from the Zhongfa Silver Company in his own car when he was suddenly kidnapped by bandits in front of the Da'an Warehouse on Zhu Baosan Road. They demanded a huge ransom for his release. Negotiations for the ransom took place in Hangzhou. After his family reported the incident to the French police, Chinese and Western detectives rescued him. Three members of the bandit gang, Zhu Jingcheng, Tang Shiliang, and Chen Zhongheng, were arrested, sent to the former French Mixed Court for trial, and sentenced to five years of imprisonment in the Western prison, after which they would be sent to the inland government for further proceedings. In the autumn of the 20th year of the Republic of China (1931), the French police arrested two more members of the bandit gang: Li Weicai from Nanhui, who was a lookout during the kidnapping, and Lu Ruowang from Shaoxing, who negotiated the ransom in Hangzhou. This led to the involvement of

Wei's Brother-in-Law

Zhao Weixian, a lieutenant colonel battalion commander of the 6th Battalion of the Independent Tax Regiment of the Ministry of Finance, who was from Zhengzhou, Henan, was found to be related to the case. At the time, Zhao's unit was stationed in Bengbu, and his family (wife, mother, wife was Zhu Baosan's ninth daughter, Ninth Miss, engaged to Zhao when he was an instructor in the Chinese Volunteer Corps) and younger brother resided in Suzhou. They learned that Zhao was taking leave to return to Suzhou to visit his family. Wei's son, Yuansheng, accompanied police detectives to Suzhou to arrest Zhao and bring him to Shanghai, where he was sent to the Second Special District Court along with Li and Lu for public prosecution. After repeated court hearings, it was determined that Li and Lu were indeed involved in the case. Li was sentenced to 20 years of imprisonment, and Lu was sentenced to life imprisonment. Since Zhao Weixian was a

Active Duty Military Officer

The ordinary court could not accept the case, and Zhao was ordered to be transferred to the military authorities for trial. After Li and Lu's sentences were finalized, they were sent to the Second Special District Prison. However, the Police Department disagreed with the Zhao Weixian part of the ruling and appealed to the Third Branch of the Jiangsu High Court. After the trial, the appeal was rejected. The Police Department still refused to concede and appealed to the Supreme Court. In April of this year, the police found Qian Lihe, a local Shanghainese who was the driver of the car used by the bandits when Wei Tingrong was kidnapped, hiding on Zhonghua Road in the South City. They immediately cooperated with the Public Security Bureau to arrest Qian and bring him to the Second Special Court for prosecution. A hearing was held, and the already convicted criminals Zhu Jingcheng, Tang Shiliang, Chen Zhongheng, and Li Weicai were brought from prison to be confronted. (Lu Ruowang was not brought because he had been transferred to a prison in Anhui.) According to Li and Zhu, Wei Tingrong had come to the police station, Guangci Hospital, and prison several times, offering them cigars, Dutch water, and candy to

Incite False Accusations

That Zhao Weixian and others were involved in the case. Subsequently, Qian Lihe was repeatedly interrogated, and due to the lack of evidence of his crime, he was acquitted. At the same time, the Police Department's appeal regarding Zhao Weixian was finalized by the Supreme Court after three trials, and the appeal was rejected. Zhao was still sent to the military authorities for review. The Military Law Department of the Songhu Garrison Command investigated the case and determined that Zhao Weixian had not committed any crime. He was declared not guilty and released, regaining his freedom. Zhao, feeling aggrieved by the false imprisonment and suffering damage to his reputation and mental anguish during the 20 months of detention, believed that it was all due to Wei's instigation and false accusations. He filed a complaint with the Command, accusing Wei. After repeated summons, Wei not only refused to appear but even detained the messenger sent by the Command. After negotiations by the Command, the messenger was released. The Military Law Department, considering that Wei not only refused to appear but dared to detain the messenger, which was unlawful, reported the matter to the former Commander Dai and

Issued an Arrest Warrant

For Wei Tingrong to be brought to justice for questioning. Now, Zhao Weixian has filed a criminal self-accusation with the Second Special District Court, accusing Wei Tingrong and his son, Wei Yuansheng, of instigating false accusations and obstructing freedom, requesting that they be brought to justice according to the law. Upon receiving the complaint, the court summoned both parties. The hearing was originally scheduled for the afternoon of the 12th of last month, but because the plaintiff had not collected all the evidence, he requested a postponement, which was reported in the previous newspaper. Yesterday afternoon at 2:00 PM, the case was scheduled to be heard for the first time in the Second Criminal Court of the Second Special Court. The plaintiff, Zhao Weixian, wearing a military uniform, military hat (made of yellow wool), and black leather boots, arrived at the court on time with his agents, lawyers Zhang Shizhao, Qin Liankui, Chen Qun, Chen Heting, and Zhou Xiaobo. The defendant, Wei Tingrong, also arrived at the court with his defenders, lawyers Chen Lu, Yu Zhongluo, and Peng Qi. Many friends and relatives of both parties and news reporters who were paying attention to the case arrived at the court to observe the hearing. The courtroom was

Crowded with People

Almost to the point of being overcrowded. Judge Li Changnian, accompanied by clerk Wang Baoxun, took his seat and summoned both parties and their agents into the court, preparing to begin the hearing. At that time, police lawyer Yao Zhaodi had also entered the court. Judge Li first asked the police lawyer why he was in court today. Lawyer Yao stood up and stated that, according to the provisions of Article 2, paragraph 2 of the Agreement, the administrative authorities of the concession could participate in the proceedings. Today, he was participating in the hearing based on that article. The judge stated that since the establishment of the court two years ago, many self-accusation cases had been tried, but no police lawyer had ever participated. Today, he was not willing to set this precedent. As for the participation mentioned in Article 12 of the Agreement, it referred to civil litigation, while in criminal self-accusation cases, Article 346 of the Criminal Procedure Law stipulates that

Public Prosecution Procedure

Matters that should be presented or debated by the prosecutor, in a private prosecution procedure, are carried out by the private prosecutor. There are no regulations for participation, but since the police lawyer has claimed participation based on Article 12 of the agreement, this judge intends to request an interpretation from a higher authority in accordance with the agreement. This case cannot be tried today, and a new date will be set for retrial, the Li judge said. After Judge Li finished speaking, Qin Liankui, the lawyer representing the private prosecutor Zhao Weixian, stated, "Directing the litigation is indeed the court's authority, but in my opinion, while requesting an interpretation, the trial can still proceed according to the usual procedures of the Criminal Procedure Law. Now that the parties are present, please call the roll." Then, Yu Zhongluo, the defense lawyer for the defendant Wei Tingrong, stated, "Regarding Qin Lawyer's claim, I also agree. Because Article 12 of the agreement concerns participation, it is a civil lawsuit, so today it seems possible to

Proceed with the Trial

Judge Li also said, "This case is a private prosecution case. Now that the police are participating, it is inconvenient to proceed with the trial." He also asked the police lawyer for his opinion. Lawyer Yao stood up and explained the purpose of his participation, saying, "Private prosecution cases in the concession often do not follow Article 337 of the Criminal Procedure Law. The reason why the police have not participated in the past two years is because they did not know the details of the cases. Now that we know about this case, we are participating in court based on Article 12 of the agreement." Lawyer Qin then stood up again and said, "My request to proceed with the litigation is based on the usual procedures of the Criminal Procedure Law, not to say that it can be tried under a

Special Organization

As for Lawyer Yao's argument that private prosecution should be limited to Article 337 of the Criminal Procedure Law, not only is the precedent of the Special District Court limited to direct infringement of individual legal rights as stipulated in Article 337, but also Article 4 of the agreement, in public prosecution cases, allows the concession administrative authority or the victim to file a lawsuit, and the prosecutor executing the public prosecution only has the right to appear in court to present the case. This permits direct private prosecution, which arises from the agreement. If the agreement is to be invoked, then Article 4 should be given priority. Please consider Lawyer Yao's cited Article 337 of the Criminal Procedure Law and my cited Article 4 of the agreement together for reference." He also stated that the private prosecutor Zhao Weixian is a military officer, and his residence is not in Shanghai proper. If the court reschedules the trial, please issue a summons early. Judge Li agreed, and then announced the adjournment. The two spectators surged out like a tide, and the self-prosecution case with three-sided disputes shook the court, each with its own reasons, and it is not known how it will be resolved in the future.

Lu Fengzhu's Appeal Case Lu Himself Was Not Present Yesterday The Judge Questioned Whether He Had Fled - Result: Trial Adjourned -

Lu Fengzhu, the manager of the Zhonghua Printing House on Xizang Road, previously guaranteed that the Da Zhonghua Printing Bureau would print more than three million Sichuan Zhonghe Bank interest-free deposit certificates, ensuring that no counterfeit certificates of the same edition would ever be discovered. A guarantee contract was signed with Zhonghe Bank. However, not long after Da Zhonghua finished printing the certificates and delivered them to Zhonghe Bank for distribution, counterfeit certificates amounting to more than 370,000 yuan were discovered on the market. The Sichuan authorities arrested Wang Hongbin (who introduced Zhonghe and Da Zhonghua to sign the printing contract), and seized more than 50,000 yuan of counterfeit certificates. Wang confessed that these counterfeit certificates were printed in collusion with Lu Fengzhu, Xi Youtao, the manager of Da Zhonghua, Chen Yiting, and his brother Wang Zhian. Wang was immediately executed by the military. Meanwhile, Zhonghe Bank appointed Zeng Bing as its representative and hired lawyer Tan Yigong in Shanghai to file a lawsuit against Lu, Xi, Wang, and Chen in the First Special Court for forgery of documents. A judgment was reached, and Lu Fengzhu was sentenced to two years of imprisonment. In addition to the original guarantee that he would be available whenever summoned, he was required to post 3,000 yuan in cash as bail. Lu refused to accept the judgment and hired a lawyer to appeal to the Second Branch of the Higher Court. Yesterday morning, Judge Zhao Zhengtang of the Higher Court opened the court to summon him, but Lu Fengzhu did not appear. His representative, lawyer Peng, appeared in court. Judge Zhao immediately declared to the appellant's lawyer that, according to the bailiff's report, when he went to Lu Fengzhu's residence to summon him, the person living with him said that Lu had been on the run for two weeks. News reports also stated that Lu had escaped, which further proved it. Was Lu indeed evading justice? Lawyer Peng immediately stated that the defendant had gone to Moganshan to recuperate and was not evading justice. Future summonses should be sent to the Zhonghua Printing House, which could forward them. Moreover, the appellant is a member of the Chamber of Commerce. If he wanted to escape, he would definitely not waste public funds by hiring me to appear in court. The court should convict based on the law, but it only knows how to determine whether the defendant is guilty according to the law. His status is not something the court wants to hear about. Moreover, after the original trial, his written guarantors all went to the court to withdraw their guarantees, and they did not hand him over to the court, which shows that the appellant had a tendency to flee. Now, based on the bailiff's report that he has escaped, this court should arrest him according to the Criminal Procedure Law. However, lawyer Peng insisted that the appellant would definitely appear in court and that there was no danger of him fleeing, and he presented a medical certificate from a Western doctor as proof. The court asked if the lawyer could guarantee that the appellant would appear in court, but lawyer Peng could not take on this responsibility. Judge Zhao then announced that since the appellant Lu Fengzhu had not appeared, the case would be rescheduled for trial.

Impersonating Officials and Defrauding People Arrested Pretending to Search for Opium Dealers Two Criminals Arrested, One Escaped

Xu Huihao, a 50-year-old man from Hangzhou, runs a hotel and lives at No. 3 Ronglu Lane, Mayuan Lane, in the city. Xu is addicted to opium, so he has a set of opium paraphernalia at home. At about 2:00 PM the day before yesterday, two men suddenly broke into Xu's house. One was wearing a Western suit and had a short beard, and the other was wearing a traditional Chinese gown. They claimed to be officers from the Municipal Public Security Bureau and said that they had received a report that Xu's house was privately setting up a gambling den and trafficking opium, so they had come to search it. Xu, seeing that these people were imposing, did not dare to argue and allowed them to search each room. They found a set of opium paraphernalia and immediately wanted to take Xu to the Public Security Bureau for interrogation. Xu was shocked and begged them to spare him from being taken to the bureau. The men then said, "We are here to search under orders from above. Now, considering that you are a legitimate businessman, please give us 50 yuan, which we will take to the bureau to help you out. Otherwise, there is no way to avoid punishment." At this point, Xu realized that the purpose of these people was to extort money. He pretended to comply and asked for a reduction in the amount. As a result, they agreed on 15 yuan, to be paid at Xu's house between 6:00 and 7:00 PM that evening. The men then left. Xu reported the situation to the Second Precinct of the First District, and patrol officer Hu Qiuqiao and police chief Li Fuyi were dispatched to disguise themselves as workers and wait at Xu's house. At about 7:00 PM that evening, the men came as agreed to collect the money. The police immediately stepped forward and arrested them. However, another man who came with them took the opportunity to escape. The two men who were arrested were taken back to the precinct. Yesterday morning, when Director Liu conducted a preliminary hearing, one confessed his name as Xu Zupei, 25 years old, a local, living at No. 3 Yongchang Road, Lan Nidu, Pudong. The man wearing the Western suit confessed his name as Zhang Pingjiang, 28 years old, from Shanghai, residing at No. 26 Yuanyuan Lane, Route Ghale, French Concession. The one who escaped was named Lu Jinsheng. The rest of their statements were evasive. Xu and the others were accused of daring to impersonate public officials and extort money, which was extremely illegal. An official document was prepared and they were sent to the Municipal Public Security Bureau for interrogation.

Three People Suffocated by Coal Briquettes Tragic Change in the Yu Tongjin Family The Subletter Suspected Discovery

Yu Tongjin, a 35-year-old man from Ningbo, used to work as a partner on a ship. His wife, Xu, was the same age as Yu, and they had two daughters, the eldest named Qidi, 9 years old, and the youngest named Shandi, just 4 years old. The family lived together in the kitchen lean-to at No. 15 Cihui Fang, Xilin Road, outside the West Gate. The night before last, Yu went to another port with the ship and has not yet returned home. His wife, Xu, lit a coal briquette stove in the room and cooked dinner on the stove, which she ate with her two daughters. Then she closed the doors and windows tightly and went to bed with her two daughters. Because the weather was a bit cold, she did not extinguish the coal briquette stove, intending to use it for warmth. Unexpectedly, at about 11:00 AM yesterday morning, the subletter of the house, Wang Xiaogui, and others still did not see Xu and Qidi get up, and they became suspicious. They knocked on their door repeatedly, but there was no answer. They then managed to break open the door and saw the mother and two daughters lying on the same bed, their faces pale and lifeless. They went forward to touch them and found that their bodies were ice-cold. The coal gas in the room was very strong and made people nauseous. Wang and the others were shocked and believed that Xu and the others must have been poisoned by coal gas. They reported the situation to Director Li of the Second District General Office. Because the matter concerned human lives, he ordered the head of the Fifth Tu to report to the Shanghai Local Court to conduct an autopsy. At about 4:00 PM, Prosecutor Xiao and others, who were commissioned, arrived at the scene for the autopsy and determined that the deceased, Yu Xu and her two daughters, had all died of coal gas poisoning. The bodies were handed over to the head of the district to notify her husband, Yu Tongjin, to come to Shanghai as soon as possible to prepare coffins and collect the bodies. After the autopsy, they returned to the court.

Doctor Qu Shaoheng Expresses His Opinion on the Tian Yu Lawsuit From a Theoretical Perspective

Lawyer Tian Heming sued Doctor Yu Songjun for negligence in his practice, which caused the death of his wife, Ms. Tian Gu Linyi, after childbirth due to dysentery. The details have been recorded in this newspaper. Now, Doctor Qu Shaoheng has studied the case from a theoretical perspective to determine whether Doctor Yu should bear legal responsibility. His statement is very insightful. The original text reads: "November 1, 1933, Shanghai Shen Bao, carried a news item about lawyer Tian Heming suing Doctor Yu Songjun. After carefully reading the full text, the reasons stated in his complaint can be divided into two points: (1) The mistake of using ice on the postpartum woman (in obstetrics, after childbirth, she should be called a puerpera); (2) The negligence of not disinfecting the enema, which led to death from dysentery. I am in the medical field, specializing in obstetrics, for 18 years. I have been in Beiping and have been in Shanghai for less than a year. I have no acquaintance with Doctor Yu Songjun. I may not hesitate to make a fair judgment from a professional point of view, for the reference of the medical and legal fields, with no emotional influence mixed in. It has been a long time since obstetrics in our country has been underdeveloped. In recent times, with the gradual spread of Europeanization, a ray of light has begun to appear. After the establishment of the National Government, there was a clear determination to improve midwifery, and there were clear regulations restricting old-fashioned midwives. However, for five years now, there has been no significant progress. One is due to the lack of social awareness, and the other is due to the lack of government protection. The responsibility of an obstetrician is heavier than any other department, because it is related to the lives of both mother and child. Therefore, there are particularly many medical disputes related to obstetrics, especially in our country, where the government has no protection and society has no right or wrong. There are few doctors who do not walk on thin ice. Society can be blind, the law can also be blind, but academics must not be blind. This is why the attitude of a third-party scholar is so valuable. In my opinion, the Tian Yu lawsuit can be discussed in several points: (1) Can an ice pack be used for breast swelling? (2) Can an ice pack applied to the breast cause diarrhea or reduce overall resistance? (3) Did Gu Linyi die of dysentery? (4) Besides the transmission of dysentery through the enema, is there no other way? (5) Did Gu Linyi die on the ninth day after being discharged from the hospital, and should the responsibility be borne by Doctor Yu? (6) Is it medically accurate to say that if there is no disease three days after childbirth, then the puerpera's danger period has passed? (1) Can an ice pack be used for breast swelling? Milk is secreted by the mammary glands. The amount of milk depends on the strength of the mammary gland's secretory function. The strength of its function can be controlled by artificial methods. There are two ways to reduce it: (1) Chemical methods, i.e., applying medication; (2) Physical methods, such as ice packs. Ice packs are widely used in new medicine. In internal medicine, they are used to relieve fever and clear the mind. In surgery, they are used to reduce inflammation and relieve pain. In addition to the scope used in internal and surgical, obstetrics also uses them to stop bleeding. When human skin is exposed to the cold air of an ice pack, blood vessels constrict, blood flow slows down, swelling decreases, and the pressure on the nerves is reduced. Moreover, the nerves themselves become dull due to the stimulation of cold air, so the function of the organs is also reduced. Applying an ice pack during breast swelling is legal in terms of academic theory and facts. However, people in our society often criticize new medicine's use of ice packs, in a word, because they lack scientific (do not understand the conduction and dissipation of physical heat) common sense. (2) Can an ice pack applied to the breast cause diarrhea or reduce overall resistance? Exposure to wind and cold can cause diarrhea and reduce resistance. An ice pack is harmful if it is used improperly. Moreover, if the patient feels uncomfortable, he will not allow it to be placed for a long time. However, if it is used properly, the patient will feel comfortable and will not reject it. Gu Linyi had an ice pack from around 11:00 AM on August 3 to 3:00 AM the next morning (August 4). If she felt uncomfortable, she would not allow it to be placed for 16 hours. Since it was used properly, there is no reason to reduce resistance. If it is said that the cold air from an ice pack applied to the breast can be transmitted to the abdomen, then how can the direct placement of ice packs on the abdomen in cases of appendicitis, peritonitis, and gastrointestinal bleeding be explained? (5) Did Gu Linyi die of dysentery? Dysentery is indeed an infectious disease, but what Chinese people call dysentery often refers to ordinary chronic enteritis based on a slightly increased number of bowel movements and symptoms of tenesmus. New medicine's so-called dysentery must have infectious pathogens such as Shigella or amoeba. Does lawyer Nan Heming's claim that Ms. Gu Linyi had dysentery based on the results of a medical examination, or is it just based on the common customs of so-called dysentery in a broad sense? If there is no medical examination to confirm it, it cannot be designated as an infectious disease in law. (4) Besides the transmission of dysentery through the enema, is there no other way? Regarding Gu Linyi's dysentery, whether it is bacterial or amoebic, the source of the pathogen is still worthy of study. According to the usual practice, most of them enter through food. Why doesn't lawyer Tian Heming pay attention to food and only refers to the transmission of the enema? Yu Songjun is a formal doctor and should not lack the common sense of disinfection. The Zhongde Hospital is also one of the few obstetrical hospitals in Shanghai, regardless of whether its equipment is good or bad (I have never been there). I think it is unlikely that there is no sterilizer for the enema tube. Lawyer Tian's reference to the transmission of the enema must have seen something. If there were patients in the hospital at the same time as Ms. Gu who had true dysentery, whether the enema used was used by that patient, whether it was disinfected, and whether it was immediately applied to Ms. Gu, it is not difficult to prove the contrary. Gu Linyi died on the ninth day after being discharged from the hospital, and should the responsibility be borne by Doctor Yu? The Chinese people's faith in doctors is very weak, especially in new doctors. It is common to see that when they first seek medical treatment, they praise them to the skies, no different from immortals. If the medicine is not effective immediately, they become suspicious. If the symptoms are in the middle of their course and seem a little heavy, they change their minds and repeatedly change doctors. If they unfortunately die, they do not examine the condition of the body, the virus, or the doctor who treated them, as if their name has fallen off the list of successful candidates and the article is full of flaws. Gu Linyi moved to Tongde because she had diarrhea for three days in Zhongde, which is the common nature of the Chinese people. However, since nine days have passed since she left the hospital, and the patient began to deteriorate, should the progress during these nine days also be attributed to the former doctor? There is room for research on this from both a medical and legal point of view. It is difficult for doctors to be responsible for the safety of their patients' lives when they diagnose and treat them. (6) Is it medically accurate to say that if there is no disease three days after childbirth, then the puerpera's danger period has passed? Puerperas are no different from ordinary women. The diseases they get, in addition to a few special diseases, can also be suffered by ordinary women. Typhoid fever, diphtheria, scarlet fever, and other infectious diseases can all take the opportunity to invade. Why is dysentery unique? Does the so-called disease within three days only refer to puerperal wound infections, that is, puerperal fever? However, the incubation period of puerperal fever also varies depending on the type of pathogen. It is not a true statement in line with academic facts to say that the danger period of a puerpera has passed if there is no disease three days after childbirth. Combining the above points, Doctor Yu Songjun has his own reasons for not being responsible for the death of Gu Linyi. Lawyers can sue, and doctors can also testify. Fortunately, we in the medical profession can seek out the truth and correct it with a scholarly attitude."

Literary Figure Zhang Jumo Passes Away

Mr. Longshui Zhang, whose literary name was Jumo, the secretary of the Sino-French Pharmacy in Shanghai, was a top disciple of Mr. Feng Junmu of Cixi. He was skilled in calligraphy and writing, and he enjoyed a long-standing reputation. He successively served as a teacher in schools in Ningbo and Shanghai and as an editor in newspapers. His novels were popular. In addition to his job, he supported himself by selling his calligraphy. Recently, he suffered from pulmonary disease due to overwork and died in his residence in Ningbo on November 1 at the age of 51. Mr. Zhang had great ambitions in his youth. He studied at the Hangzhou Military Academy and secretly plotted revolution. The head of the academy, the Manchu San Duo, wanted to harm him. He changed his name and hid in Cixi, devoting himself to literature, and ultimately ended his life in this way. He was honest and self-disciplined throughout his life and lived a pure and unworldly life. After his death, he was destitute and had no food at home. His friends Chen Bulei, Guo Xuanqian, Chen Hanwen, Ren Shigang, and others planned to raise funds to support his surviving family. There are many old friends of Mr. Zhang in Shanghai who are willing to donate money. Those who wish to donate can contact Zheng Weizhang of Yuan Maosheng Cotton Cloth Store on Nanjing Road.

The branch distributed exquisite leather wallets to guests and depositors as souvenirs. It is said that Chuan Xiao'an, Du Yuesheng, Zhang Xiaolin, and others have returned to Shanghai yesterday.

Taikang Company's New Factory Expands Greatly

In recent years, the imported biscuit industry, seeing the great activity of the domestic biscuit industry in our country, has set up factories in Shanghai with new-style machines and huge capital from industrial countries, both to get rid of the shackles of tariffs and to be a strong enemy of domestic goods. Nanjing Road Taikang Canned Food Co., Ltd. has occupied a long history of more than 20 years in the domestic food industry. Its biscuits, sweets, and canned foods have been deeply recognized by the Chinese people. Now, in order to compete with foreign merchants, the company is spending a lot of money to add a large-scale manufacturing plant in Fenglin Bridge, South Shanghai. The content and equipment are planned by design experts, so it is particularly complete. All of the 1933-style large biscuit machines have been purchased from the Yingpeike factory. The machine can produce tens of thousands of pounds of biscuits per day and is indeed the best tool for production. The biscuits produced by the machine are already on the market, and the quality and taste are better than imported ones. (The picture in the middle is of the factory building)

Hunting Prohibited Near Forts

Jin Zhishang, a maintenance worker at the Wusong Forts, reported that hunting has traditionally been prohibited near the forts. However, recently, foreign residents have frequently been seen carrying guns and ammunition, freely firing shots while hunting, even late at night. These foreign residents are not only violating the prohibition, but there is also deep concern that misunderstandings may arise in the future. Therefore, he has reported this to the Songhu Garrison Headquarters, which will forward it to the municipal government for prohibition to prevent accidents. It is understood that the municipal government, questioning how foreigners could arbitrarily hunt within the garrison area, has already instructed the relevant authorities to take measures to prohibit such incidents whenever they occur, to avoid misunderstandings and prevent unforeseen events.

Special District Court Announces the Course of Illness of Western Prisoner Bossack: Mayor Wu Sent Zhang Tingrong to Investigate Yesterday; Bossack Only Requests Transfer for Treatment

Fuxing News Agency reports that the English-language Minle Weekly recently sent a letter to Mayor Wu, published in the newspaper, stating that an Austrian doctor named Bossack had been detained by the Second Special District Court for committing a crime and sentenced to a fine of 1,000 yuan. Bossack was unable to pay, resulting in imprisonment, which led to a serious illness. If he is not transferred to a hospital, his life will be in danger. They specifically requested the Mayor to find a way to provide relief. Since the publication in Minle Weekly, Mayor Wu has paid great attention. He specifically sent a letter to the British editor of Minle Weekly, Mr. Bowman, to come to the Municipal Government for discussion and asked Mr. Bowman to provide evidence. If this is the case, he will find a way to help. A reporter from Fuxing News Agency feels that this matter is sudden and has a significant impact on the reputation of the court and international relations. Yesterday, he specifically inquired about the details, which are recorded below.

Reason for Imprisonment

Yesterday, the reporter from Fuxing News Agency first visited Ying Shi, the President of the Second Special District Court, to inquire about the reason for the Austrian's imprisonment. According to the President, Bossack, some time ago, using the pretext of opening a hospital, committed fraud against a Chinese man named Wang Maoting, obtaining 100,000 yuan in foreign currency. After the incident came to light, he was arrested by the police and brought to the court for trial. The court sentenced Bossack to repay Wang Maoting the money and pay a fine of 1,000 yuan. At that time, Bossack, unable to pay the money and without anyone to vouch for him, was sent to the detention center.

Already Ill

Initially, after the police arrested Bossack, they discovered that he suffered from diabetes and sent him to the prison ward of Guangci Hospital for treatment. During the trial, because Bossack's illness had not healed, he was still returned to the prison ward of Guangci Hospital after the trial. After the verdict, the detention center also deemed Bossack's illness to be very serious and immediately sent him to the prison ward of Guangci Hospital after receiving him. The claim that Bossack was critically ill in prison and would lose his life if he was not transferred to a hospital is somewhat exaggerated.

A Glimpse of the Prison Ward

After meeting President Ying, the reporter from Fuxing News Agency obtained the consent of Gao Xiaoxu, the warden of the detention center of the Second Special District Court. Gao sent a guard to accompany the reporter to the prison ward of Guangci Hospital to investigate Bossack's condition. The prison ward is a Western-style bungalow with a fence surrounding the front of the eaves, resembling an animal enclosure in a zoo. The ward is quite large, facing south and sunny, with a large square lawn outside the door. The air is fresh and circulating. The ward houses five or six sick prisoners, with Bossack being the only Westerner. The prisoners all lie on iron beds, covered with clean bedding, similar to a third-class hospital ward.

Bossack's Own Account

The reporter from Fuxing News Agency met with Bossack under the eaves of the prison ward. Bossack, speaking in French, stated that he suffers from severe diabetes, with his urine sugar level having increased from 29 degrees to 39 degrees. His nerves have also been severely stimulated and are extremely disordered. He is now only seeking a transfer for treatment and is also requesting not to be confined in the same place as Chinese people, so as to avoid loneliness and depression due to language barriers. Bossack also said that he has a wife and five children living at 1086 Yuyuan Lane. However, since his arrest, the family's livelihood has lacked support, and he fears that they will soon become starving. Bossack spoke with tears in his eyes, and the scene was extremely tragic.

Mayor's Attention

Mayor Wu paid great attention to this matter. Yesterday morning, he specifically sent the intelligence director Zhang Tingrong to the Second Special District Court and the prison ward of Guangci Hospital to conduct detailed investigations separately. Zhang also personally asked Bossack what he wanted from the Mayor. Bossack replied that he only wanted a transfer for treatment, so that his mental disorder could gradually recover and his diabetes could hopefully be cured. Zhang promised to convey this to the Mayor and find a way to help him, and he comforted Bossack, telling him to be quiet and abide by the law.

Haikingburg Circus Feeds Animals This Morning

Mr. Shi Huide, the general manager of the Haikingburg Circus, announced that today is Sunday, and there will be three performances as usual, at 2:30 PM, 5:30 PM, and 9:15 PM. Ticket prices are the same for each performance. Starting today, animal feeding will also be held every Sunday at 11:00 AM. This will surely be welcomed by those who love wild animals. Previously, animal feeding was not held on Sundays. In the future, the feeding will be suspended on Mondays. In this way, visitors to the zoo on Sundays can also witness the real-life situation of lions, tigers, leopards, and bears competing for food. Among the new programs, the most exciting ones include at least three acts: one is Mr. Kaideng's amazing mixed wild animal performance, one is the airborne acrobatics of the McCombs brothers, and one is the "White Qimei" team's skills. The most amazing of all is Mr. Kaideng, who leans into the cage of giant lions, tigers, and black bears in the arena for a mixed performance of lions and bears, with the black bears standing upright and demonstrating the lightness of their feet. The success of this kind of mixed animal act is due to him being the number one in the world. In addition to these, the other 20 major acts are also very worth seeing. Anyone who has visited once will have an unforgettable impression. Even the several equestrian performances alone are worth the price of admission. Four beautiful women perform interesting equestrian skills, and Haikingburg's equestrian skills are also pleasing to the eye. What Crime is Committed by Buying and Selling Children? Lu Lindi's Statement Vividly Depicts the Scene

Yesterday afternoon around 2 PM, Hou Xiaowen, a police chief from the First District of the Municipal Public Security Bureau, found Gao Shousheng, Xu Silin, Qian Axin, and Changzhou women Jian Dengshi, Zhou Wushi, etc., with a girl, preparing to board the Huaan ship berthed at the Datong Wharf in Nanshi. Their appearance was suspicious, so he brought all six men, women, and children to the district. During the preliminary hearing, District Chief Guan Gong took the case. According to the girl, named Lu Lindi, she is 14 years old and lives at No. 47, Oujia Road, Beishi. A few days ago, while playing in front of her house, a man named Wang abducted her to No. 53, Xingli, North of the Nicheng Bridge, in the home of his mistress Qian Dengshi. Then Qian Dengshi took her to Gao Shousheng's home. Now Gao wants to take her to Fujian, etc. When questioned, Gao Shousheng confessed that he is 46 years old and lives at No. 55, Rishengli, Lima Road. Lindi was bought from Wang Daajie (i.e., Qian Dengshi) for 90 yuan. He has now resold her to a Fujian man named Lin, and the price has been set at 120 yuan. Therefore, today, he was helping her to Datong Wharf to board the Huaan ship and set off for the Lin family in Fujian. Because there were many people, they could avoid the attention of the police, so he invited Xu Xiaolin to accompany them to the wharf. Unexpectedly, they were still discovered by the police chief, leading to their arrest. Xu Xiaolin and others gave evasive statements. Considering that the matter concerned the abduction and sale of people, they were ordered to prepare documents and send them to the bureau for further investigation.

Education News Sports

Jiangda Football Match Schedule Arranged Regulations Also Published

The Jiangda Football Championship, with the participation of eight universities, is scheduled to begin on the 11th of this month. The regulations are recorded as follows: (1) A single round robin system will be used; (2) Each time, the winning team gets two points, the losing team gets zero points, and a draw gets one point each. If the total scores are equal, another game will be played. If a draw is encountered, it must be extended for thirty minutes. The dates and referees will be designated and hired by the committee; (3) The rules of the game will be implemented according to the football rules of the National Games; (4) The referee will be hired by the home team, but must be approved by the visiting team. If both parties cannot agree, they may request the committee to hire; (5) If the venue is not suitable due to rain or if it is absolutely necessary, the game may be rescheduled. The date will be notified to the visiting team by the home team, with their consent (the makeup game must be held before December 31); (6) If a team does not appear on the field within fifteen minutes of the scheduled game time, it will be considered a forfeit, but if an accident occurs en route that forces the selection, it will not be counted; (7) The winning team must report the results of each game to the chairman of the football committee within two days; (8) After each game, the two teams must send the names of the players and referees to the chairman of the football committee by mail; (9) The list of players must be sent to the chairman of the football committee for review before November 11; (8) The schedule is listed below (each game starts at 2:30 PM);

November 11th
