Amateur Musings

Are Humans Worse Than Beasts?

— Gongpu

A week ago, this reporter took the time to attend a lecture at the Chinese Arts and Crafts Society given by a "Haijingbo" circus troupe's expert animal trainer on "How to Train Wild Animals." Ten days prior, I had also spent six big silver coins to see a circus performance, and I was deeply impressed by how well-trained many of the wild animals were, how obedient they were, how they followed rules, and how they maintained discipline as a group. I deeply admired the trainer's methods and regretted not knowing anything about how to train wild animals. Therefore, upon learning of the lecture at the Arts and Crafts Society, I resolved to attend. The result was very satisfying and thought-provoking.

The animal trainer's speech mainly described the personalities of various animals. He said that sea lions are the most obedient of all animals, while horses, contrary to what we might think, are very difficult to teach. Other wild animals like lions, tigers, bears, and elephants also have their own individual personalities and characteristics. The most important thing to keep in mind when training them is not to teach them actions that go against their personalities. Instead, you must build on their unique characteristics to develop their personalities. This is the first principle that anyone training wild animals should know.

Next, he discussed training methods, saying that you must have patience and follow the teaching methods, drawing on your personal experience, to gradually implement basic movements, complex training, and continuous practice until they are proficient and make no mistakes. But the main point is to be clear on reward and punishment, and the trainer must fully gain the trust of each animal. However, gaining this trust is not easy. You must constantly make the animal pay attention to your actions, so that it can gradually understand the trainer's love, and then you can train it in various performance techniques. This is the second principle of animal training.

After listening to this animal trainer's speech, I had many thoughts and doubts. First, I deeply felt that "Haijingbo" and others are not only animal training experts, but are educators in every sense of the word. We know that the various animal training principles described above are not different from the principles of many modern educators. The difference is that these principles can be applied to animals that are unreasonable and whose wild nature can erupt at any moment, whereas the education of human beings, the so-called "lords of all creation," does not fully adopt these two major principles of developing personality and gaining trust. In fact, there are many methods that fundamentally violate these principles in the schools that educate our people. Another difference is that if the animal training expert does not follow these educational principles, the animals will not be trained, will resist, and the circus cannot be performed, fundamentally violating the purpose of doing business. As for the purpose of modern school education, it is to educate young people to adapt to the environment of the existing political and social system, and to develop personality and freedom of belief. Although these are the educational principles that should be implemented, they are not suitable for the current environment and system. Therefore, although the educational principle of developing human personality is reasonable, it cannot be put into practice!

If we further ask why the educational principle of developing personality is not suitable for the current political and social system, the question is very simple. It is because the current system is largely built on a foundation of inequality. Human personalities always oppose inequality. Therefore, the more fully human personalities are developed, the more intense the resistance to the unequal system will be. Those who want to maintain the unequal system understand this key point very well, so they apply the principle of developing personality very carefully, and they are unwilling to lightly attempt it and tie their own hands. As for why this kind of education that violates personality cannot be applied to animals but can only be applied to humans, it is because human personality, although strong, is hidden very deep, and it requires full education and environmental enlightenment to be developed and expanded. Therefore, except for a few people who are born with slightly stronger personalities or who have been stimulated by special environments, most people are easily dominated by the environment and material things, and become a part of the existing environment, becoming characters without personality and without belief.

There is also a small feeling that "docility is not necessarily intelligence." We see that horses are more docile than many wild animals, but their intelligence is not very high. Nowadays, there are some people who hate people with personality and praise the unambitious and submissive, or the so-called docile. If this continues, it will ultimately turn all Chinese people into horses. However, horses are not valued in the eyes of animal training experts, because they are unintelligent fools whose personalities or wildness have been submerged!

The No-Marriage Doctrine of 30,000 Female Workers in the Outer Postal Agency

— Translated by Ms. Shuangping

Correspondence from Shunde, Guangdong

In my rural life, what I hate most every morning is the siren of the silk factory. Little did I know that this siren is a symbol of the life of the women in the whole village.

Speaking of silk factories, there are more than a hundred in our south, with an average of six to seven hundred female workers crammed into each one.

Page 20

They endure the torture of foul air from morning till night, sitting upright on a stool, facing a pot of boiling water and a pot of cold water. Their backs are close to the hot pipes. Their hands, scalded by boiling water, are attacked by cold water again and again. Therefore, their hands are always wrinkled like a monkey's face, and rough like rose branches. Their faces are pale from the sweat, their lips are blue-black, and their wet clothes stick tightly to their bodies and cannot be taken off. Especially, their eyes are surrounded by smoke and cannot see clearly, so they become useless in middle age. Their eyes have to follow the running silk thread. If they are not careful, and there is one more or one less cocoon, the silk thread will be thick or thin, and you can forget about getting your full wages. In front is water vapor, and behind is heat, creating a "climate that is different in one's own body." The young ladies and ladies who only know how to dress in red and green will never realize the hardships of the owners of the manufactured goods!

The factory owners' harsh punishments are truly countless! The factory's penalty rules are as follows: work starts at 6:00 AM every day. If you are ten minutes late to the factory, you will be locked out. It is bad enough that you won't get paid for the day, but to deduct one day's wages as a warning is the most unreasonable thing! As for the harsh punishments for silk that is reeled too thick or too thin, they are beyond description. If you argue even slightly, you will be unconditionally dismissed. After being dismissed, the factory will send a notice to all the neighboring factories. At this time, the dismissed female worker must either leave her hometown to look for work, or she will be unemployed forever!

Secondly, the foremen's barbaric oppression and insults are also commonplace for the female workers. If you are young and beautiful, or good at flattering, then no matter how thick or thin your silk is reeled, you will never be penalized; but those old women and female workers with pale faces must always be careful about losing their jobs. Even if they are not unemployed when the cocoons are on the market, the unreasonable harsh punishments and the foremen's bestial insults are already enough to make them suffer! Ah! The foremen know how to enjoy themselves. They often seek the pleasure of the female workers—playing with them, stroking their faces and breasts!

They have no courage to resist at all, but sometimes they are oppressed to the point of being abnormal—such as when the foremen take brooms and firewood to beat the female workers, then, as the saying goes, "Even the Buddha will strike fire." They swarm together like bees to make a disturbance, or rush to the machine room to turn off the main switch—called "stirring up the clams," or cut off all the silk on the machines—called "bamboo silk chicken." But no matter what kind of commotion they make, it can only last for five minutes. When the factory issues a threatening announcement, they swarm back to that terrible living hell—the factory. This is a self-employment introduction return.

Ms. Pu: Please come to No. 4 Daxilu between 2:00 PM and 4:00 PM every day to contact Ms. Li. (Initiated by the Shanghai Tuberculosis Sanatorium Main Branch)

Because there are only a few silk factories in one or several villages, the female workers who cannot leave their hometowns have to submit! Those who do not return to work are only those female workers who have been injured, lying in bed groaning, and have no money to seek medical treatment. Especially unfortunate are those who have been dismissed by the factory on some pretext!

They have a strange idea and doctrine, which is the no-marriage doctrine. The 60,000+ female workers cannot avoid being influenced by feudal heredity. Except for those who have to support their parents and children, the rest, whose families are a little more economically sound, will accumulate their daily wages. These people are also the ones who adhere to the no-marriage doctrine, accounting for 50-60% of the total number of female workers. The reasons why they do not marry are: first, the continuation of customs; second, they are economically independent. Therefore, even if some female workers have been married off by their parents, they will still try their best to get rid of it, which is called "not falling into the family." Some will also take their accumulated sweat and blood wages to redeem their bodies.

Each of those unmarried female workers has a same-sex lover; they live together as if they were husband and wife, or a dozen or more female workers live together in a house (commonly known as a "grandma's house"). In short, the female workers' adherence to celibacy is nothing more than a reflection of their oppression by capitalist society.

Life

I Murdered Someone

— Gushui

The Unemployed

My state of mind is unusually empty, and I can't seem to think about anything. If I were to furrow my brow and think all day about how to deal with my problems, perhaps my mind would become numb and fall into a state of madness. So, recently, I have been confining myself in a small room, abandoning all painful thoughts, and living a life of self-deception. My heart is as dark as a zombie.

That afternoon, my friend Qingshan appeared in my room with a smile. I was annoyed that he was disturbing the peace of my soul, but he immediately burst out, "Mr. Zhu called me and told me to let you know that a clerk is needed somewhere, with a monthly salary of thirty-five yuan. Do you want to do it?"

My heart, which had been dull and gloomy for a long time due to unemployment, suddenly lit up as if it had seen a glimmer of light. I became excited and asked, "Is it true? What did Mr. Zhu say?"

"He told you to think it over first and go see him tonight. I think this job is doable. Anyway, you're just sitting around doing nothing. It's good to earn thirty or forty yuan a month."

"Okay, but being a clerk is also a very hard job!"

"There's no way around it. It's really not easy to make a living these days!"

So my friend went back, leaving me with this small amount of joy and luck.

That night, I hired a rickshaw to go to Mr. Zhu's place. He was my teacher when I studied at a school before. Because I had a very good relationship with him at that time, he has always cared about me since I left that school and wandered for three years. This time, I came to Shanghai from afar again. On the day I first arrived, I visited his home. He treated me to a meal and even specially bought two catties of aged wine to drink with me. His sincere feelings for me have really changed from a teacher-student relationship to a friendship.

When I entered his house, I was greeted by Mrs. Zhu, who greeted me warmly like a kind mother and led me to Mr. Zhu's room. When Mr. Zhu saw me, he asked, "Did Qingshan tell you?"

"He told me, but I'm afraid this job will be very hard, right?"

"It's nothing much, probably just drafting some documents and copying things every day."

"What kind of work will he be doing? How much will he be able to earn a month?" Mrs. Zhu also asked Mr. Zhu with concern.

"A clerk somewhere, with a monthly salary of thirty-five yuan."

"Asking him to do such a humble thing is too unsuitable!"

"Sigh, what can we do! Nowadays, it's difficult to earn this much! To tell you the truth, there are four or five people who have asked me to recommend them for this position, and there are more than a dozen who have written letters to apply for it themselves. You really don't know how many people there are looking for a job these days. There are as many as crucian carp crossing the river."

"With Gu Jun's talent, it's a pity to do this kind of thing."

"Although it's a pity, there's no way around it. It's dangerous if you don't find a way to make a living first. Future hopes will have to come slowly. Nowadays, I don't know how many people like you are being suppressed by the times in this social stratum!"

"I don't think it's a pity at all. If you don't have food to eat, what hope and future are you allowed to talk about?"

"Then you can go to the office tomorrow. I'll give you this business card so they can recognize you when you get there. Be careful about everything and do your duty first. Let's talk about it after you've worked for a while."

So I said goodbye and left. After spending a relatively pleasant night, I changed into a more presentable set of clothes the next morning and went to the office.

When I arrived, I handed Mr. Zhu's business card to a man with a pair of large glasses, a handlebar mustache, and a large cigar in his mouth. He said very nicely and asked me to sit down at a desk and pointed out many things to me. For a moment, my desk was filled with files, official papers, draft books... many unfamiliar things. That was considered the start of my work.

The man then brought over more than a dozen letters, saying that they were all applications from people who wanted to take my position, and asked me to reply to them one by one. I read them all through one by one. I was stunned for a moment. It was as if there were more than a dozen sorrowful faces, faces that seemed to be expecting something, all looking down on me. I also seemed to see that all of them were followed by a group of wives and children, people who had been crushed by the pressure of life. As I wrote letters to reply to these people, I felt as if I had become a murderer, and a few tears couldn't help but well up in my eyes.

At five o'clock in the afternoon, I left the office and slowly walked home, my heart feeling as if it was carrying a thousand pounds of pain, and my throat felt as if something was stuck in it.

"Shanghai in 1933 is a place full of tragedies, and China in 1933 is a country covered in suffering—" I thought to myself, and muttered, "Thirty-five, thirty-five..."

On Words

Is It Possible Not To Work For Japanese Employers?

— Chen Caiyun

Several months ago, whenever I passed by the new site of the Japanese Marines headquarters on Jiangwan Road, which was under construction, and saw many of my compatriots working under the supervision of Japanese soldiers carrying guns, I couldn't help but think of this not-so-small question: "Why do they have to work for the enemy?" Of course, I believe that anyone with even a little bit of backbone would feel the seriousness of this question! Or some people might say: "These people are all laborers and have not received any education, so they lack a concept of the nation!" However, I can assert that there are quite a few of our educated compatriots who work for Japanese employers; and it is not only in one corner of Shanghai that this is the case, but also in Tianjin, Qingdao, Hankou... In short, in any commercial port where the Japanese have influence, this phenomenon can be found everywhere!

We don't need to talk about those traitors and unscrupulous merchants who have lost all conscience, but those compatriots who work for the Japanese are definitely not all without conscience, right? They wouldn't all recognize the enemy as their father, right? So, what is the reason why they work for the Japanese?

Once, I happened to ask a Chinese person working in a Japanese agency this question, and his answer was: "If I don't work for the Japanese, will society give me food to eat?" This sentence sounds a bit unreasonable, but upon careful consideration, there is some reason in it. If he leaves his Japanese employer, there will be people in society who ridicule him, but there will be no one who sympathizes with him. Even if there are, they will only be those who are "willing but unable" individuals! As a result, he can only join the ranks of the unemployed! Therefore, if society cannot find a way to solve their livelihood problems, it cannot but blame them for their actions!

I am not defending my compatriots who work in Japanese companies, nor am I encouraging people to work for the enemy. I am only hoping that society can do more to help this kind of person. Patriotism is a duty that everyone should fulfill, but no one can love their country on an empty stomach!

International Broadcast

Soviet Humanism

—

In the Soviet Union's first five-year plan, the development of waterways occupied a very important position. The Soviet Union has a vast land area with crisscrossing rivers, and there are many large rivers that flow for thousands of miles. The extensive use and transformation of old waterways and the excavation of many new waterways will open up many new areas for national industrialization; for the large-scale transportation of bread, raw materials, kerosene, machinery, building materials, etc., it will open up many new roads, and it will create more favorable conditions for the economic and cultural construction of various border areas and backward areas. The completion of the first five-year plan has given the Soviet Union a new look, and has brought about great changes in the Soviet Union's waterways. One of the largest engineering projects for artificial canals in the five-year plan was the excavation of the White Sea-Baltic Sea Canal.

This canal connects the two seas—the Baltic Sea and the White Sea—and is 227 kilometers long. In November 1931, the Soviet government decided to dig this canal and entrusted the work to the State Political Security Bureau. This was the starting point for the excavation of the White Sea-Baltic Sea Canal. At the end of June of this year, Yegoda, the deputy chairman of the State Political Security Bureau, made a report to the Soviet government on the creation of this artificial canal:

"The White Sea-Baltic Sea Canal, which began construction at the end of November 1931, has been completed by June 20, 1933. This means that the creation of a very large canal only took one year and nine months.

The People's Committee of Waterways has carefully examined all the equipment of the White Sea-Baltic Sea Canal, and all the dikes, sluice gates, hydro-electric technology, etc. have been done very well. Now the Soviet People's Committee of Waterways has accepted the White Sea-Baltic Sea Canal from the Political Security Bureau and has included the canal in the Soviet Union's navigable waterways. From now on, the Soviet Union has added a new waterway.

The success of this canal has shortened the distance to the Soviet Union's most important northern ports by four times. Previously, the sea route from Leningrad to Arkhangelsk was 2,840 nautical miles long. Now, thanks to the success of this canal, the sea route has been shortened to 674 miles. In addition, previously, to go from the Baltic Sea to the White Sea, it was necessary to pass through the ports of many countries, and to travel along the coast of Scandinavia. Now, thanks to the success of this canal, Soviet ships in the north can completely navigate domestic waterways without having to pass through foreign seaports. The success of this canal has provided convenient access for the development of the north's forests, timber, minerals, and natural resources, and has greatly promoted the development of the north's productive forces."

In the socialist Soviet Union, the speed of development of productive forces is unimaginable to any capitalist country. Due to the rapid development of productive forces, the demand for waterway transportation has also increased dramatically; therefore, the Soviet Union pays more attention to the development of waterway transportation than capitalist countries.

Social Anatomy Room

Individualism in Modern Society

— Zhu Anshi

Individualism is a product of the private ownership system. Human society, since the collapse of primitive communism, soon established the dominance of private ownership. Through the feudal society to the modern capitalist society, everything is built on this private ownership system, with private ownership as the foundation. Therefore, individualism has become the focus of these societies. However, in the feudal era, because social relations were not complex, although serfs were subordinate to the lords and became vassals, the lords still guaranteed the lives of serfs to a considerable extent. Therefore, the color of individualism was not very strong. But in the capitalist era, the situation is completely different. Not only are social relations very complex, but the existence of only exploitative relationships between individuals. Besides, the so-called freedom is just the freedom of private property. In short, at this time, individualism is not only very obvious, but also exceptionally developed.

Therefore, individualism is the principle of modern capitalist social organization. It is individual-oriented and individual-centered. It only recognizes the individual as the only real thing, and society is just a means to achieve individual goals. Thus, it fundamentally ignores the organic relationship between individuals and believes in the independent existence of individuals. As a result, all social rights become a clearly defined inviolable territory of individuals.

This concept is the direct opposite of the so-called socialism based on society. Because the standpoint of social centrism recognizes society as the only real thing, it does not recognize the independent existence of the individual. Moreover, the individual is only meaningful as part of the entire society, and the individual's purpose should also be integrated into the purpose of society. Therefore, if the economic organization is constructed under this principle, then the society has the responsibility to guarantee the economic life of each individual member, and in order to achieve this goal, a public agency is established to manage the production and distribution of social wealth. Therefore, this kind of social relationship is a rational social relationship.

However, in an individualistic, individual-centered society, society does not recognize the necessity of guaranteeing the economic life of each individual. The production of wealth is based on the individual's intentions, and the distribution is also based on the individual's intentions. This leads to the so-called free individual behavior of mutual exchange and buying and selling. Therefore, the economic activities of each individual in this society are not dominated by conscious and planned, but are individualistic activities conscious of their own economic interests. Each individual is based on his own position, without interfering with each other, and cannot be violated by others. It can be said that they stand on a relationship of mutual antagonism, opposition, and competition. Society itself is also generated as a result of this individual conscious activity. Therefore, individualism can be said to be the essence of modern society.

However, in this kind of society that is individual-oriented and recognizes its own selfish activities, and embraces liberalism towards the pursuit of profit, the result is the absence of control over production and distribution, an economic anarchy. At the same time, it causes the result of economic chaos in society, and allows the economically superior to dominate and exploit the economically weak almost endlessly. That is to say, capitalists, based on their individualistic selfishness and greed, not only extend the working hours, but also try their best to make the workers do strenuous labor to satisfy their private desires. Therefore, the economic freedom of activity and the private property system deny the right to survival of the members of society. All the miserable things such as unemployment, hunger, and crime will accompany the development of capitalism, and the economic panic that comes with the development will become more and more serious.

Exploitation

Career Exploration

Personality and Vocational Success

— Dr. He Qingru's Lecture, Notes by Zhang Shugeng

There are two major factors in the constitution of a career: (1) People, (2) Things. Vocational success must first have the matching of "people" and "things." Doing one thing to the highest degree can be said to be vocational success.

To reach the realm of vocational success, personality must be paid attention to the most. I often see many people who are a pity, because their lack of personality makes their career fail. There are many practical examples that can be found among our relatives and friends, either because of a bad temper, or because of a bad personality, or because of incompatibility with colleagues, which hinders him from continuing to serve.

Personality is a term that combines the reaction to "people" and to "things." What is his attitude towards me, what is my attitude towards him? What is his behavior towards me, what is my behavior towards him? Personality is not a single term, but a term composed of language, behavior, attitude, and concept.

Which personalities are successful? Everyone has different classifications, and there are more than dozens or hundreds of kinds. I will not be able to finish speaking for days. Now I will bring up and discuss a few kinds that are most related to success and do not contradict the road to success:

(1) Creation To succeed in a career, you must have a personality to create a career. For example, a carpenter became rich by making chairs, so the second, third, and fourth people set up factories to make chairs, which ruined the chair market. In fact, if you find a new path, you can also achieve the same victory as him. My meaning is not to not be the same as others, but not to be the same as others in everything without creating "new" methods.

(2) Sincerity It doesn't mean that not lying is sincerity; sincerity is like doing one thing, no matter how big or small, there will always be a result, and one point of effort will always have one point of result. Do everything seriously, whether it is big or small, serious will get a good result, and not serious will get a bad result; you must take into account the relationship of cause and effect, and do not do things sloppily. It is impossible to want to gain without working, or to want to do it in the easiest way. One point of labor, one point of price; you must use labor in the right place and concentrate on one thing.

(3) Experiment There are many things that need to be tried many times to get their results, even hundreds, thousands, or tens of thousands of times. Ordinary things cannot be successful once, so you must have an experimental attitude. The spirit of experimentation is very related to vocational success.

(4) Cooperation There are two necessities that a person must deal with when working outside: (A) natural forces, (B) man-made forces, and they must cooperate with them to succeed. For example, if a construction engineer does not cooperate with natural forces, such as using raw materials without investigating the climate and terrain, his work will definitely fail; if he does not cooperate with the foremen, he will not be able to build successfully.

To develop personality, it is necessary to have the corresponding preparations to be done: (1) Take a look at myself, analyze myself, what are my strengths? What are my weaknesses? What are my specialties? What am I lacking? (2) Analyze what kind of personality is needed in the job I want to do, and then compare the two aspects to see what I lack and what I am good at, so that I can talk about development.

Industrial and Commercial Knowledge

How to Make Blue-Black Ink

— Ouyang Guanyu

Preparation: First dissolve ferrous sulfate (Fe SO4) in 400 c.c. of cold water; then mix tannic acid (Tannin), gallic acid (Gallic Acid) and gum arabic (Gun Arabic) and dissolve in 500 c.c. of distilled water, then store in a large glass bottle, then inject ferrous sulfate solution, and quickly add hydrochloric acid (Hcl), then take 100 c.c. of water and a liquid formed by dissolving coal and carbolic acid (Phenol), stir continuously and add to become black ink.

The required amount of each liquid is: 27 grams of tannic acid, 6 grams of gallic acid, 8 grams of gum arabic, 30 grams of ferrous sulfate, 7 grams of hydrochloric acid, and 1 gram of carbolic acid.

Note: (1) Carbolic acid is poisonous. If you are not careful when manufacturing, the skin will rot if it is touched. (2) If you want to make blue-black ink, inject a small amount of Aniline Blue when stirring at the end, otherwise the writing will be black.

Biography of Famous People

Mussolini's Youth (4)

— Ms. Yan Jingcao

"Are you okay?" the policeman asked him.

"Are you okay?" he also asked the policeman.

"What are you doing here?" the policeman said.

"I'm guarding the printing equipment, you know that!" he said.

"Get up!" The policeman's face suddenly became stern, and Mussolini had no choice but to yawn a few times and follow the policeman away.

In this way, Mussolini entered the prison. In a small detention center, accompanied by an old, disabled, and filthy criminal, he spent several days of carefree and unfree life.

Long-term wandering gradually made Mussolini's thinking tend towards revolution. He arrived in Geneva, where he spent a lot of time, and was able to associate with writers and politicians. These people all admired his talent, ambition, and perseverance, so they were happy to associate with him. At that time, he could often write articles for Swiss and Italian magazines, and sometimes give speeches on socialism and international affairs. Not only did he win the sympathy of the labor class, but also intellectuals were moved by his words. At this time, he had already begun to attack "democracy", so the Swiss authorities paid close attention to his actions and secretly monitored him at any time.

However, Mussolini did not hide the sharpness of his thoughts and words because of the surveillance of the Swiss government. His actions were still as intense as before, inciting and making trouble everywhere. The Swiss police believed that this young radical was detrimental to the so-called security of the republic, and ordered him to be deported. So Mussolini had to flee to Lausanne, where he wrote a letter to his friend Dr. Weiss (DAWyss), who was the representative of the Socialist Party in Geneva:

"I just got a message from a Geneva newspaper that you are preparing to petition the Swiss Confederation to withdraw the order to expel me from the country - this order was proposed by the chief of police. I have a very short autobiography, which may be narrated for your reference. I came to Switzerland at the age of nineteen, and at first worked as a proper worker in Lausanne. Later, I returned to Italy to visit my mother, and soon lived with my friend Danatini, who was a political prisoner, in Annemass, on the French border. In this place, we wanted to start an 'international socialist review', but it was not successful. On March 1, 1904, I went to Geneva to register at the university; they will definitely tell you that I am an anarchist, which is completely untrue. In recent years, I have written many writings and speeches, and I have donated money to the Common People's Daily in New York, the Labor Struggle Daily in Lugano, and the Pioneer Daily in Milan. From these actions, to be honest, the police cannot find any anarchistic materials. In Switzerland and Italy, I am considered a socialist. Once, the proposal I put forward at the Zurich conference, although very revolutionary, cannot be determined to have an 'anarchistic color'. I wasted forty days in Geneva, spending most of my time in the university library. The police wanted to add a few strokes to their merit books, and simply dragged me into the net of crime, which is their usual trick; however, none of the reports are true. After I received this eviction order, I wanted to return the key to the room, clean up my belongings, and discuss with my lawyer; but they forced me to leave without explanation. The authorities told my lawyer that I had returned to Alimasi, which was a trick they deliberately used to deceive people, fearing that the lawyer would argue. In fact, I was forced to take a car to Josso, and then rush back to Italy. Only then did I realize the true face of the Republic, and simply threw aside the false signboard of the Republic guaranteeing freedom. This expulsion is not only a disgrace to the Republic, but even if the same event occurred in a monarchy, it might be an unconscious act! Now I am in Lausanne, hoping not to be oppressed by them again. I think that police chief wants to justify himself, I am afraid it will not be easy!"

From this letter, we can know that the wandering and helpless life of Mussolini, this poor young man, in the past few years has made significant changes in his thoughts and actions. At this time, Mussolini was no longer a naughty wild child, nor a young, energetic, and patriotic soldier. He was a hard worker who sought happiness for the poor, and also a young man who was eager to learn, and also participated in the organization of socialists. Although he was inevitably expelled by the Swiss government, he did not lose heart because of this.

Film Special Issue

Interview with Chinese Film Artists (18) (Continued from Last Month's 28th)

— Shaji

(8) Zhang Shichuan, Director of "Remnant Spring" (Part 1)

Regarding this gentleman, I think many people know that he is a giant in the Chinese film industry. Why? We only need to know him in his business; he is the controller of the Star Film Company, but at the same time he is also an artist. An entrepreneur and an artist, the combination of the two, his greatness is conceivable.

Because of his greatness, he must be a capable person, and because he is a capable person, he must work hard. Therefore, it is only now that I can get an opportunity to interview him in his busy schedule.

I really feel ashamed that for such a small matter, I actually bothered him to abandon all his official duties and run from the second floor to the director's department to meet me.

If we believe in the techniques of the Jianghu physiognomists, then looking at his face and figure, we can decide that he is a great nobleman. Look, his fat face, his short and thick body, is simply a complete big flower face. That whole body of meat is really well cultivated, and every bit shows his good fortune. He is already very developed now, and will continue to develop in the future. Although he does not have to be a first-rank official, he has at least developed the aura of being carried by eight people. This kind of aura is very amazing.

After a lot of nonsense, it is now time to record his conversation.

"Mr. Zhang went to Nanjing to film the National Games. What good opinions do you have about the National Games?" This is what I asked. I only heard him say:

"The results of this year's National Games are very good, and there are many athletes. Many events broke the national records. However, it is much worse than the Far Eastern Games and even worse than Japan. However, because some athletes have difficulties in life, they cannot solve the problem of eating and cannot practice sufficiently. However, there are many promising athletes among them. If they can continue to work hard with a stable life, they will definitely have good results in a short time. Therefore, I hope that the government authorities should be able to allocate a sum of money to stabilize their lives and allow these athletes to continue to practice. Now it is said that Liu Changchun is paid 100 yuan a month, and many others have nothing. I think it is better to arrange those good athletes into various government departments. Suppose there are 100 people, it only costs 100,000 yuan, which is a very small number for the government, but next year's Far Eastern Games and the 24th National Games will be very promising. ..."(To be continued)

Film Review

Review of "Too Much Harmony"

— Ling He

Too Much Harmony

—Paramount Production, Premiered at Da Guangming—

I watched the British "The Chance of Night Time" the day before yesterday, and then I watched "Too Much Harmony" yesterday. Because the stories of the two are quite similar, it is not impossible to mention them at the same time. For example, the former "The Chance of Night Time" tells the story of a lawyer who changes a wife one night, and the latter "Too Much Harmony" also writes about a young couple who give up their original lovers because of their emotional compatibility and finally reconcile. The two have the same theme; if you find a better object than your original lover before marriage, you should get the one you love.

It goes without saying that this kind of leisurely work does not express reality in a positive way. However, comparatively speaking, "The Chance of Night Time" is much more substantial in terms of the implicit aspect of the story and its horizontal development. Generally speaking, British films are different from the frivolousness of American films, and another example can be found here.

Isn't it? In this film, we can only see some so-called gorgeous appearances. Due to the appearance of the so-called All Star Cast, we certainly cannot ignore its business methods of using this as a selling point. On the other hand, the producer's caution in the production of this film can also be glimpsed at the same time. However, this all-star team is not as successful as the all-star team of "Grand Hotel." This does not mean that all the stars here are second-rate stars, but that at least in terms of content, it is not as tasty as "Grand Hotel."

Therefore, merely exaggerating the form cannot increase the value of the work, not to mention that the performance is not perfect. Here we can explain more specifically; the screenwriter wants to make Losue and Eddie divorce, and uses all means. The old lady of the song and dance troupe destroys it from the middle. It further explains that she wants to engage in destruction, not out of reluctance, but by adopting a method of revenge. This point is very commendable in writing skills. However, the author made a clumsy attempt to teach a person to impersonate the son of the match king, and Losue actually believed it, which is too childish. As for writing the vain Losue, because she knew the son of a rich man, she resolutely terminated her engagement with the vocalist, which is quite realistic.

In addition, the author unfolds the love scenes of the male and female protagonists in the play, subconsciously indicating that this is just a theatrical love. However, this is always an unexpected gain for the author.

The above is a review of the script, and in terms of performance, we have the following opinions.

The director has used the most modern dance forms as much as possible, fully demonstrating the American film's madness for form. Among those dance scenes, the most brilliant one is naturally the last one that uses "wind." However, this is just saying that he is more crazy about selling the temptation of flesh. If American films, in addition to these self-abandoning scenes, what else can show his characteristics?

Because the director's control over the actors is not very appropriate, and at the same time, he must make every star have a role to play, so we have not seen any actor with a unique performance here. Even for the male and female protagonists, in addition to the male protagonist Bing Crocby having a sonorous voice and the female protagonist being able to be so quiet, there is almost no better performance. However, for the two of them, it is slightly inferior to the "College Student's Humor" that was shown at the same theater before.

As for the scenery, we saw several very valuable stage devices. For example, the night scene at the bridge, the store layout, and the falling flowers blowing in the wind add a lot of color to this film.

"Blood Road"

— By Manqian

— Central Cinema —

In the past, apart from the so-called "Big Three" film companies, smaller-capital producers often took a different path due to a lack of equipment and talent. For example, since the transformation of the film industry last year—in other words, since the major companies began focusing on "realistic subjects"—many of the smaller producers continued to produce fantastical works to capture another segment of the audience.

However, the newly established White Rainbow Film Company was able to recognize its own mission and resolutely produce this work with anti-imperialist significance. Although it was not very successful, we should admire this perseverance.

"Blood Road" tells the story of an unemployed worker who seeks help from his father-in-law, a treacherous merchant, due to the burden of his family, but is rejected. As a result, he is forced to take the risk of becoming a thief. This illustrates the increase in unemployment, the ruthlessness of treacherous merchants, and the ever-expanding dark side of society. Later, a love story is inserted: the fiancée surprisingly sympathizes with him and leaves her family. After he is released from prison, she lives with him. Although the insertion of the love story does not make the whole play seem loose, the woman's change is a bit inexplicable. In the end, the worker joins the Volunteer Army. The play ends in a rather tragic scene.

The director often uses scenes with very dim lighting. Two shots are particularly worth mentioning: one is a "tracking shot" of dozens of workers carrying iron plates, and the other is a "medium shot" of Wang Chunyuan and a dozen other workers gathered together. It has a very New Russian flavor. The flickering of the light is undoubtedly due to the poor equipment. Among the actors, Qin Haha is the most moving. He exceptionally plays an impoverished old man, and his movements and facial expressions are very capable of touching the audience's heartstrings. Wang Chunyuan's movements are suitable for the identity of a worker, but his facial expressions are insufficient. As for the female lead, Qian Siying, she is a complete failure; neither her crying nor her smiling makes people feel any sincerity. The treacherous fat worker with one big eye and one small eye, although he does not have many scenes, leaves a deep impression on the audience. Therefore, the success or failure of an actor does not depend on whether they are a "main character" or a "minor character," but on whether they can fulfill their responsibilities in the role they play.

In short, "Blood Road" is still a very immature work, in terms of script, director, actors, photography, and set design. However, to encourage many of the emerging small producers, the reporter has lowered the standard and written this article.

"The Technique of Love"

— Review of Moore

Marry Me

— Grand Theatre —

American films occupy a "dominant" position in the Chinese market. This is true not only commercially but also in terms of audience interest. Therefore, many people find the more restrained British films uninteresting. In reality, the British are more conservative, so they do not "exaggerate" (or develop to the extreme) in various aspects of filmmaking.

Not developing to the extreme does not necessarily mean in terms of technique. Even with regard to the social function of film, they do not develop it, (naturally, subjectively, it is still beneficial to themselves).

"The Technique of Love" is a typical British film. Of course, "The Technique of Love" has many operatic elements. However, every British sound film has some operatic elements. This is the first point.

Secondly, British films often have a bit of humor added, and "The Technique of Love" is itself a comedy. Therefore, it does not necessarily rely on the actors' performances to make people laugh; the story itself is interesting.

However, "The Technique of Love" is revealing. It says that the young Robert does not love his colleague Anhen, but loves the banker's daughter Qina because he has long wanted to "obtain a wealthy daughter to get rich." Even later, when he "resolutely marries Anhen," it is only because "Anhen went to Robert's apartment to perform the duties of a housewife, and for a time, the trivial matters in the apartment were in good order," and it was only at the suggestion of Robert's two younger brothers.

In today's society, love is originally gilded, but some people insist on embellishing it, saying that "love is unconditional and supreme." Now, because the truth is too obvious, it can no longer be embellished. Therefore, it is also reflected in "The Technique of Love." He is openly admitting it.

In the past, I have seen many British films whose shots change very little. Often, there is a frontal medium shot, a close-up, and a long shot. Other close-ups, etc., are rarely used. The angles are also almost the same: a frontal view, a side view, and then a frontal view, rarely even using overhead or oblique views. This kind of shot and angle are suitable for filming musicals because musicals are inherently neat. As for ordinary films, the first thing to do is to be realistic. Therefore, the shots must follow the actors' free performances and change accordingly. Although the shots in "The Technique of Love" do not change as much or as strangely as in American films (naturally, unnecessary changes are not right), they are not as rigid as in many British films.

Moore was widely welcomed in "Happy Marriage" because of her excellent performance. Even in "Spoiled Darling", which she co-starred with Imogen Stubbs, she also gave many extraordinary performances. Here, whether she is playing a young girl who is infatuated with love, or a calm and patient young girl, she is able to convey the mood of the character to us through her expressions. I think it is very commendable!

"Sacrifice" Filmed on Location at Zhenru

— Ming

The interior scenes of the Lianxing Film Company's "Sacrifice," including the male and female dormitories, have been completed, and the dock exterior scenes were also completed on the 30th of last month. Yesterday morning around 10 o'clock, the company went to Jinan University in Zhenru to shoot exterior scenes. A group of more than ten male and female actors arrived at the location and were suddenly surrounded by hundreds of students eager to watch the filming process. After Director Lu Shi and the director of student affairs of the school requested, the encirclement was lifted, and they began filming the entrance to the female dormitory and the students going to and from class. It is said that "Sacrifice" is set against the background of promoting the patriotic enthusiasm of overseas Chinese students and young people across the country, and also focuses on the tense situation of Jinan University students participating in the anti-Japanese war during the "January 28th Incident." Therefore, the school believes that this film is of great significance for promoting education, so it has specifically allowed it to be filmed as a background and is doing its best to assist in the completion of the film. (Que Chou)

Novel and Film Feast No More Dinner at Eight (5)

— Ma Teng

Oliver Jordan, because Carlotta Vance was going to sell her stock, thought of Packard. Packard used to be just a miner, but now he has money and mixes with financiers and presidents. Today, he invited him to his office to ask if he would be willing to help the Jordan Company in this time of economic panic if the need arose. Packard appeared to be nonchalant. Perhaps he was willing, but his words were very evasive. He wanted to see the list of shareholders first. What if Carlotta's stock was sold to him? ... What if he really bought enough of Jordan Company's stock? ... Fostick, the old manager of the Jordan Company, who had been working since his father's time, did not trust that Packard at all. He said! "I can't trust Packard any more than I can trust pulling the cow's tail to knock the cow down." Fostick's words were insightful, but Oliver hoped that his insight was wrong ... In this difficult time, he had to believe someone ... he had to ask for someone's help ... Where could he find this person? And there was tonight's banquet. That boring Fincliffe and his shrewish wife ... But Carlotta would definitely come, she was still so witty and charming ... Perhaps he could talk to her and stop her from selling the stock ... Packard would also definitely come. With diplomatic means, he might be able to establish a personal friendship ... Perhaps Packard could help him by bailing him out. ...

In Packard's house, in Kitty's dressing room, Kitty looked at her new makeup in the mirror, her heart full of happiness. Packard ran in and said beside her, "Okay. Jordan's stock has been bought, bought under someone else's name." He stretched his sleeves and said, "I'd pay a thousand dollars to see Jordan walk into the meeting room on Monday when the shareholders meet, and see Baldridge and Weston each holding a large roll of stock. What kind of expression would he have on his face!" After he finished speaking, he put his hands in his pockets and confidently returned to his own dressing room.

Kitty sat quietly without saying a word, lost in thought. Packard wasn't the only one with ambition in the world. She also knew what methods to use to get what she needed. Like her husband, she was good at using means to seize what belonged to others and make it her own. When her husband came in again, she cunningly said, "I guess this is the last time Jordan invites us ... If he finds out that it was your trick, how can he not hate you?" Packard snorted and said, "Tch, how would he know? It's all arranged. Hah, who do you think I am!" He paced around her room again, full of confidence. Kitty glared at him and said, "You're so clever, you'll end up in jail one day!" Packard nonchalantly said, "It's too early to put me in jail. They've been watching me since I was in Montana. But I got Cooper Hill, and I got Ema. Then I came to New York, and they all belonged to me. Heh, whose wife has a man with such big balls?" He looked at the diamond bracelet on his wife's soft jade arm. (To be continued)

Home
